文书的书写流程是怎样的呢？文书写作是在开始申请之前，由我们的专业文书导师跟你进行 1v1头脑风暴，深度沟通之后结合你的背景为你量身定制文书，初稿完成之后会交给你，你可以反馈意见，老师继续进行修稿直至定稿。所有文书都是我们最终确定定稿之后才投递。

单单希望文书提升录取概率在申请硬件背景已经确定的情况下，例如gpa、原来的院校、活动经历等因素已成定局无法改变，文书是唯一可以由申请人掌控的可变量因素；一份好的文书可以提升录取记录，但是如果您的硬件没有符合学校要求，再好的文书都没有办法帮您获得录取的；以上的结论是通过我们多年的经验以及入驻招生官的专业从业意见。
订购的是文书，却希望老师在选校、网申等方面提供咨询服务文书需要的讨论都是必要的亲，如果是职业规划/网申服务就属于半DIY咨询了，因为我们本身只是作为平台保证服务顺利进行，导师也是按照用户订购服务类型进行工作哈，请知悉哦！
服务有效期是什么意思有效期是指开始到完成的服务期限，约束用户、导师双方在合理时间内完成交付和售后服务。这个时间也可以根据申请人的详细情况进行协商的。
推荐信细节操作您好像不是很清楚提交推荐信的流程。首先我们在填网申时把老师的邮箱填上保存后，老师会收到一封要求帮助提交推荐信的邮件，邮件里有链接用户名密码。通过这个老师才能提交推荐信。大部分都是通过网推，极少部分是邮寄。邮寄也需要老师签字。学校那么多教过你的老师，找1-2个，说说好话。我们这边很多学生，跟教授商量的都是自己写好，拿给教授修改，这样也给他们减少麻烦。
文书不会使用模板吧？您好，WordSunny 提供的是申请文书专属定制式服务，所有的信息都是根据您本人的实际情况进行深度挖掘，换言之，文书专属于您。
使用文书，申请不上怎么办？您好，留学申请是一个综合的考察结果，其中包含成绩、实习经历、原学校背景、文书等因素，文书只是其中的一项，并不是录取的唯一因素；文书的判断标准在于是否符合申请院校要求以及申请人的实际经历，所以并不保证录取的，您请理解。:)
文书特点我们的特点是灵活以及专属，所有的信息都是根据您本人的实际情况进行深度挖掘，换言之，文书专属于您。文书一稿常规完成时间为收到素材后72小时，但是这期间可能存在的讨论以及信息获取会有所浮动，另外如果导师需要更多时间打磨文书，交付时间导师也会与您协商的。
超值文书套餐包含什么超值文书套餐包含申请规划+背景提升+1所学校全部文书及选校评估+1篇简历服务；申请规划、背景提升及选校定位都是通过一对一语音咨询的形式进行；然后再开始处理文书。文书可以由导师代为完成，或者学院跟导师一起完成即学员在导师的指导下完成初稿，导师修改直至定稿。
标准文书套餐服务流程1. 学员填写信息素材搜集表；2.导师根据素材表跟学员头脑风暴，挖掘经历，分析申请学校要求，确定文书大纲；3.完成一稿；4.互动反馈直至定稿。
标准文书套餐包含什么标准文书套餐包含1份PS/SOP，2-3份推荐及1份简历。可以由导师代为完成，或者学员跟导师一起完成即学员在导师的指导下完成初稿，导师修改直至定稿。
学生一直问问题，不愿意花钱/一直问问的客户应该如何应对WordSunny运用共享经济的原理，帮助同学们找到对口的有经验的过来人，就可以和行业大牛面对面答疑解惑。泡论坛一周，可能不如过来人几句经验之谈，花钱买时间，用几十上百元，就可以帮您节省一周甚至更多的时间。我们服务的核心是找到“过来人”，能够根据自己的实际经历和经验来帮助学员解决的问题，您现在所有遇到的迷茫困惑，本身就是申请导师服务中需要解决的，这个问题也并不是一两句话能说清楚，这需要大量的调查分析，然后制定相应的解决方案。就像医生看病，并不能通过前台的接待和咨询就解决医疗本身的问题。
大一需要评估/或者信息不够，比如绩点不确定服务中心回复您目前的背景暂不具备申请竞争力评估的条件。 现在开始如果我们要做服务，首先需要协助您规划职业方向，然后锁定三个档次的申请目标院校，在实际定位中会略高于背景，因为您可以目前具备的准备时间可以给您带来的提升可能性较大。在截止申请递交前，我们会在您已经既有的背景基础上，对您进行有目的、科学的、有规划的包装，例如参加财务相关的实习、数据建模、比赛等活动。在此期间还我们的服务导师会继续指导您提升课业成绩、标化成绩。在申请过程中，作出合理的陈述，挖掘您的潜在优势、亮点，打动申请院校。
对自己背景不自信-服务亮点提炼/定位回复策略（大三/大四接近申请季的学生）我们对您的申请目标和您的背景对比了服务中心的数据库，初步评估您申请XXX学校的竞争力可以达到七成，硬件条件本身不是问题，但与您竞争的，是和您一样具有同样背景或是更好背景的同学，他们一样985/211，课业成绩佳、经历丰富，学习能力强。在这样的情况下，我们作为机构，其中很关键的因素，是需要给您配备一位有经验、有同样专业留学经历的申请导师，利用既有的时间，指导您有针对性的、高效的提升背景；在申请过程中，科学的包装、合理的陈述，深度挖掘您的申请优势和亮点，打动申请院校。
害怕强制申请学校我们有制约条款，选校报告需要得到客户确认，才可以进入下一个申请环节，选校不满意可以申请取消服务。另外制约条款也是约束双方的，选校是根据学员的实际背景和学校录取要求、结合我们的录取经验进行选择的；申请竞争的核心是申请人本人的竞争力，我们做的核心工作其实是挖掘和提升（条件允许的情况下）。
对保底学校比较排斥申请选校方案是一个策略性很强的工作，冲刺、适中和保底的策略是导师给学生制定的一个科学的组合方案；根据实际条件，保底并不意味着低排名；一切都是根据事实为基础做出的科学判定。
我们做什么如果只是按照GPA、语言成绩等标准指标来选择学校，只需查询官方要求，即可知道是否符合学校要求的；但是除了标准的流于表面的录取要求之外，每个学校都有自己的特有的招生偏好。例如申请人的潜在的学习能力、领导力、逻辑思维能力等等，每所学校要求都不尽相同，而且这额要求都是录取委员会评估的标准，但是并不会放在官网说明。这些都是我们的专业导师做的。
嫌费用高比我们便宜的肯定不止一家，淘宝还有几千块的（针对半DIY），我们的服务是精准匹配相关领域专业导师，导师从业经历丰富。中介的文书导师一般都是大专或者本科英语毕业的，但是我们的导师全是有海外经历的硕士以上的常青藤导师。这肯定是没有可比性的哈。
选校方案，我可以一起参与吗同学你好，我们是按照你的背景给我们评估委员会，评估后给你一套方案，按照冲刺+适中+保底的方案，这些院校也是结合我们的数据中心给出的评估，最后确认学校和专业，我们是一起决定，不是机构已方决定。
申请不成功是否有退费使用WordSunny导师的经典选校方案：保底+适中+冲刺，如果申请没有录取可以紧急补申3~6所，所需费用由WordSunny承担。您也可以选择申请退费，退还全额服务费。我们去年一站式服务是100%拿到offer的，请放心，口碑就是咱们的生命线，我们的努力绝不会小于您，您拿到offer了对于我们也是极大的宣传。
服务过程中，有几位老师一站式服务采用5位1体的服务模式；首先申请主导师会通过一对一在线课程的形式进行选校定位，包括背景提升计划、申请专业可行性分析、目标院校分析及推荐；并根据申请人背景及确定的学校个性化完成文书；此外，外籍文书导师会对文书进行润色。申请主导师会同时指导学生准备申请材料，如果成绩单、学位证、毕业证、在读证明等的翻译，或邮寄（如果需要的话）并辅导申请人完成网申。接下来会进行模拟面试，签证，行前指导。
一站式服务的解释1、WordSunny从申请国家、院校、领域等方面精准的匹配到您申请所需要的导师，导师结合自己的经验会协助您完成从背景提升、规划、选校、文书到最后签证、海外学习生活等方面的事物。WordSunny提供的是顶尖的资源对接而非某一项服务。2、一站式申请服务会根据申请人的背景进行职业规划，按照规划和已经具备的硬件要求来制定院校定位，在有限时间内最大化提升录取背景，量身定制文书，个性化写作及辅导，针对院校的模拟面试等等，到最后的签证，海外学习生活指导,都是非常重要的服务项目。一站式申请不但服务全面，导师顶尖，而且全程自主参与，过程可见、可控。
父母对线上不放心？我们 WordSunny 和传统的留学中介不一样，是一个留学平台，把国内外有留学背景或相关行业领域的导师与想申请留学的学生联系起来，这些导师不仅懂留学，而且还会给申请者关于行业职业的深刻看法。WordSunny成立于2011年，主要靠的就是口口相传，口碑和高质量服务才是让平台一直都生存到今天，很多人已经给 您体验过，使用过，如果不好我们肯定不存在了，您说是不是？
跟传统线下中介的区别1、你要这么想，我们的导师都是在国外常春藤读书或者是已经毕业于顶尖学校的，他们的专业度你应该可以想象到的，我们平时所接触的机构里面真正有几个留个学的，可能留过学的只有总监这个级别的人，那你要想总监每天事情那么多能够很好地给你服务吗？2、这是一种新型的服务模式，对于申请导师的介绍可以说是是市面上最详细的了，有背景、案例以及录制的课程，目前市面上的中介公司的顾问，几乎都没有留学经历，您对于他们的了解，也仅限于销售咨询；我们的申请导师都来自顶尖名校，利用o2o的模式提供留学咨询服务，如果把他们放在传统中介，这种层次的经历、经验，基本都是总监级别的哈，这一点您如果咨询过中介公司就会了解到的。3、很多同学对留学申请服务可能了解不够完整，认为留学服务就是帮助申请人写文书和递交申请，这可能也是市面上大多数机构做的实际工作。实际真正的留学申请服务，包含了很长一段时间。首先是在申请前应该对将来的职业有一个预设。普通中介公司顾问，可能并不具备相关行业的工作经历，也谈不上对行业、职业有深刻的认知和看法；4、不管是中介还是线上的咨询平台，本质上来说都是为学员提供留学咨询服务，帮助学员申请到理想的大学；从目前市面上的中介公司，约90%的顾问是没有留学经历的，更别说专业对口了，没有留过学做咨询顾问有一个比较大的问题，就是一切都只能按照中介公司和学校校代的合作来选择学校；不像校友内推的一手院校信息和专业领域内的行业消息，毕竟留学最终也是为了最终就业；比如我们有在CMU读计算机，毕业有在Facebook任职工程师的咨询导师，他会从根本上告知学员如果您将来想在硅谷工作，应该进什么样的学校、念什么书、结识什么朋友、参加什么活动、什么公司会在什么时间会在学校进行什么类型的活动、应该如何与招生面试官套辞～～等等。
同学你的背景信息我已经了解了，你需要WordSunny留学申请平台给你提供什么服务呢？是全程一站式服务。半 DIY服务。
学生背景信息方便提供一下吗？就读哪所大学？学习的是什么专业？目前大几？百分制分数是多少？有什么实习或者科研没？
线上留学中介业务?我们是最早一批做线上互联网留学平台的机构，今年已经十周年了
对公司业务有疑问？我们 WordSunny 属于线上互联网留学平台，总部在西安，不过学生都是全球各地的，这个可以放心哈(“因为我们和传统的留学中介是不一样的，把国内外有留学背景或相关行业领域的导师与想要留学的学生联系起来这些导师不仅懂留学而且还会给申请者一个关于行业职业的深刻看法。就是你申请哪里什么方向匹配的就相关方向有留学背景的导师帮你写文书哈，所以我们的导师也是在全球各地的。
如何快速拉近与客户的距离？您好，我是 WordSunny 留学申请平台的申请规划师Kevin，请问有什么可以帮您的吗?
客户初次意向咨询如何打招呼？哈喽你好呀，很高兴认识你，是有留学的打算吗，想申请哪里呢?(申请诉求：申请地区+方向+申请目的）对了，怎么称呼呢，我备注一下
WordSunny是什么？WordSunny创立于2011年，是业内首创导师模式辅导的留学品牌，总计覆盖多达 200 余个专业。申请导师均来自于世界哈、耶、普、斯等知名院校，目前已经有来自全球292所院校52个专业的3000+申请导师入驻WordSunny留学平台。WordSunny优势：导师选拔通过率为20%，平均每位导师同时只辅导5名学生，注重质量、精益求精是我们的追求。39次产品迭代，全流程服务为结果负责，无录取承诺退款。WordSunny全部评价、案例均为用户真实提供，永远不删差评。WordSunny使命：帮助客户成为具备国际化视野的杰出人才。WordSunny服务理念：行家指路，少走弯路。
你们在其他城市有门店没？我们是互联网留学公司，目前只有在古城西安。

编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan怎么样？编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7055.html；简介：本科就读新加坡南洋理工大学电子与电机工程系，并以一等荣誉学位毕业；毕业后任职于世界500强企业，也是世界上最大的油田服务公司斯伦贝谢，从事项目管理相关工作；工作过程中想转行从事金融相关工作，就着手做了两件事，第一件事报考CFA，并在2018年通过三级考试并顺利持证；第二件事是申请金融相关的研究生，因为在海外时间比较长了，对申请学校也比较了解，所以是通过DIY的方式拿到了帝国理工（IC）、伦敦政经（LSE）以及伦敦大学学院（UCL）的offer并最终选择去帝国理工就读矿产与能源金融专业；研究生毕业后，经过一年的思考并了解各类金融相关工作，最终决定加入投资行业，并选择股权投资母基金这一细分领域，且很有幸的加入盈嘉资本担任投资经理一职。能为大家提供的帮助：1、在大学期间长期担任学生社团的管理层角色，且保持了相对高的成绩，对大学生活规划有独到的见解，可以帮助学生在入校之时就规划好大学四年的生活，例如如何在社团、实习、成绩间取舍。2、毕业后从石油行业逐步过渡到金融行业，对如何转行，尤其是非金融学生如何找到一份适合自己的金融工作有深刻的认识，并能根据学生情况给出具体可实施的计划、找到适合学生的岗位并对如何准备面试等具体事项提供帮助。3、因为从事股权投资行业，所以对当下热门的行业都有所了解，例如互联网、人工智能、半导体、先进制造等，对各行业未来的趋势看的相对清楚，结合自己多年的留学经历与海外工作经历，如果你对选学校选专业有困惑，以及对自身在现有行业内的发展路径不清晰，都可以帮你更好的做出决定。目前的服务状态是不合作

编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan怎么样？编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7055.html；简介：本科就读新加坡南洋理工大学电子与电机工程系，并以一等荣誉学位毕业；毕业后任职于世界500强企业，也是世界上最大的油田服务公司斯伦贝谢，从事项目管理相关工作；工作过程中想转行从事金融相关工作，就着手做了两件事，第一件事报考CFA，并在2018年通过三级考试并顺利持证；第二件事是申请金融相关的研究生，因为在海外时间比较长了，对申请学校也比较了解，所以是通过DIY的方式拿到了帝国理工（IC）、伦敦政经（LSE）以及伦敦大学学院（UCL）的offer并最终选择去帝国理工就读矿产与能源金融专业；研究生毕业后，经过一年的思考并了解各类金融相关工作，最终决定加入投资行业，并选择股权投资母基金这一细分领域，且很有幸的加入盈嘉资本担任投资经理一职。能为大家提供的帮助：1、在大学期间长期担任学生社团的管理层角色，且保持了相对高的成绩，对大学生活规划有独到的见解，可以帮助学生在入校之时就规划好大学四年的生活，例如如何在社团、实习、成绩间取舍。2、毕业后从石油行业逐步过渡到金融行业，对如何转行，尤其是非金融学生如何找到一份适合自己的金融工作有深刻的认识，并能根据学生情况给出具体可实施的计划、找到适合学生的岗位并对如何准备面试等具体事项提供帮助。3、因为从事股权投资行业，所以对当下热门的行业都有所了解，例如互联网、人工智能、半导体、先进制造等，对各行业未来的趋势看的相对清楚，结合自己多年的留学经历与海外工作经历，如果你对选学校选专业有困惑，以及对自身在现有行业内的发展路径不清晰，都可以帮你更好的做出决定。目前的服务状态是不合作
编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang怎么样？编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7060.html；简介：拿到了香港城市大学（语言研究-翻译研究）/香港科技大学（中国文化）/比利时鲁汶大学(KU Leuven)（语言学高级硕士）/莱顿大学（语言学研究型硕士）/兰卡斯特大学（传播学）的offerIELTS （7.5），GPA: 3.3/4.0本身读的是汉语国际教育/英语，所以对语言学、应用语言学（对外汉语/对外汉语）、东亚语言文学、传播学、教育学有较多的了解现在在比利时的鲁汶，鲁汶是一个典型的欧洲大学城，几乎一半人口都是学生。目前的课程基本是深入的以研究为基础的，每一门课程都要求自己开展独立研究项目作为期末考核标准。上课人数是小班教学，每门课的人数在2-6个学生，因此在上课的时候能够和教授进行积极的互动。虽然是文科，我们还可以选定自己感兴趣的研究小组，联系老师，进研究小组进行相关的课题研究。目前的服务状态是可以受理

编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao怎么样？编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7061.html；简介：在香港一年多的时间，顺利完成学业，交友广泛，可以为学员分享香港tips和推荐稳定靠谱的房源！目前在国内top5综甲设计院工作～学长很爱交朋友，沉迷于音乐，本科时曾组建乐队，担任主音吉他手。日常会泡健身房，偶尔踢足球，喜欢旅行和摄影～学长从大四上拿了offer后，一直在做留学兼职，已成功帮多名学弟学妹拿到offer。非常熟悉香港，新加坡和英国的工科和商科专业的招生标准，申请流程，擅长为学生进行时间规划、择校和文书写作。除此之外，还可以指导学员进行背景提升、分享实习和求职经验。学员与我的关系不仅仅是服务和被服务，而是成为彼此相互信任的好友，学员入学后，在生活、学习、找实习、找工作时遇到问题都会找我咨询，我会用自己的经验和资源为学员指明方向～目前的服务状态是可以受理

编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang怎么样？编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7060.html；简介：拿到了香港城市大学（语言研究-翻译研究）/香港科技大学（中国文化）/比利时鲁汶大学(KU Leuven)（语言学高级硕士）/莱顿大学（语言学研究型硕士）/兰卡斯特大学（传播学）的offerIELTS （7.5），GPA: 3.3/4.0本身读的是汉语国际教育/英语，所以对语言学、应用语言学（对外汉语/对外汉语）、东亚语言文学、传播学、教育学有较多的了解现在在比利时的鲁汶，鲁汶是一个典型的欧洲大学城，几乎一半人口都是学生。目前的课程基本是深入的以研究为基础的，每一门课程都要求自己开展独立研究项目作为期末考核标准。上课人数是小班教学，每门课的人数在2-6个学生，因此在上课的时候能够和教授进行积极的互动。虽然是文科，我们还可以选定自己感兴趣的研究小组，联系老师，进研究小组进行相关的课题研究。目前的服务状态是可以受理

编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang怎么样？编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7060.html；简介：拿到了香港城市大学（语言研究-翻译研究）/香港科技大学（中国文化）/比利时鲁汶大学(KU Leuven)（语言学高级硕士）/莱顿大学（语言学研究型硕士）/兰卡斯特大学（传播学）的offerIELTS （7.5），GPA: 3.3/4.0本身读的是汉语国际教育/英语，所以对语言学、应用语言学（对外汉语/对外汉语）、东亚语言文学、传播学、教育学有较多的了解现在在比利时的鲁汶，鲁汶是一个典型的欧洲大学城，几乎一半人口都是学生。目前的课程基本是深入的以研究为基础的，每一门课程都要求自己开展独立研究项目作为期末考核标准。上课人数是小班教学，每门课的人数在2-6个学生，因此在上课的时候能够和教授进行积极的互动。虽然是文科，我们还可以选定自己感兴趣的研究小组，联系老师，进研究小组进行相关的课题研究。目前的服务状态是可以受理
编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan怎么样？编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7055.html；简介：本科就读新加坡南洋理工大学电子与电机工程系，并以一等荣誉学位毕业；毕业后任职于世界500强企业，也是世界上最大的油田服务公司斯伦贝谢，从事项目管理相关工作；工作过程中想转行从事金融相关工作，就着手做了两件事，第一件事报考CFA，并在2018年通过三级考试并顺利持证；第二件事是申请金融相关的研究生，因为在海外时间比较长了，对申请学校也比较了解，所以是通过DIY的方式拿到了帝国理工（IC）、伦敦政经（LSE）以及伦敦大学学院（UCL）的offer并最终选择去帝国理工就读矿产与能源金融专业；研究生毕业后，经过一年的思考并了解各类金融相关工作，最终决定加入投资行业，并选择股权投资母基金这一细分领域，且很有幸的加入盈嘉资本担任投资经理一职。能为大家提供的帮助：1、在大学期间长期担任学生社团的管理层角色，且保持了相对高的成绩，对大学生活规划有独到的见解，可以帮助学生在入校之时就规划好大学四年的生活，例如如何在社团、实习、成绩间取舍。2、毕业后从石油行业逐步过渡到金融行业，对如何转行，尤其是非金融学生如何找到一份适合自己的金融工作有深刻的认识，并能根据学生情况给出具体可实施的计划、找到适合学生的岗位并对如何准备面试等具体事项提供帮助。3、因为从事股权投资行业，所以对当下热门的行业都有所了解，例如互联网、人工智能、半导体、先进制造等，对各行业未来的趋势看的相对清楚，结合自己多年的留学经历与海外工作经历，如果你对选学校选专业有困惑，以及对自身在现有行业内的发展路径不清晰，都可以帮你更好的做出决定。目前的服务状态是不合作
编号为235的申请导师Xuecong Li 怎么样？编号为235的申请导师Xuecong Li 官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7054.html；简介：-目前的服务状态是不合作
编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao怎么样？编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7061.html；简介：在香港一年多的时间，顺利完成学业，交友广泛，可以为学员分享香港tips和推荐稳定靠谱的房源！目前在国内top5综甲设计院工作～学长很爱交朋友，沉迷于音乐，本科时曾组建乐队，担任主音吉他手。日常会泡健身房，偶尔踢足球，喜欢旅行和摄影～学长从大四上拿了offer后，一直在做留学兼职，已成功帮多名学弟学妹拿到offer。非常熟悉香港，新加坡和英国的工科和商科专业的招生标准，申请流程，擅长为学生进行时间规划、择校和文书写作。除此之外，还可以指导学员进行背景提升、分享实习和求职经验。学员与我的关系不仅仅是服务和被服务，而是成为彼此相互信任的好友，学员入学后，在生活、学习、找实习、找工作时遇到问题都会找我咨询，我会用自己的经验和资源为学员指明方向～目前的服务状态是可以受理

编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan怎么样？编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7055.html；简介：本科就读新加坡南洋理工大学电子与电机工程系，并以一等荣誉学位毕业；毕业后任职于世界500强企业，也是世界上最大的油田服务公司斯伦贝谢，从事项目管理相关工作；工作过程中想转行从事金融相关工作，就着手做了两件事，第一件事报考CFA，并在2018年通过三级考试并顺利持证；第二件事是申请金融相关的研究生，因为在海外时间比较长了，对申请学校也比较了解，所以是通过DIY的方式拿到了帝国理工（IC）、伦敦政经（LSE）以及伦敦大学学院（UCL）的offer并最终选择去帝国理工就读矿产与能源金融专业；研究生毕业后，经过一年的思考并了解各类金融相关工作，最终决定加入投资行业，并选择股权投资母基金这一细分领域，且很有幸的加入盈嘉资本担任投资经理一职。能为大家提供的帮助：1、在大学期间长期担任学生社团的管理层角色，且保持了相对高的成绩，对大学生活规划有独到的见解，可以帮助学生在入校之时就规划好大学四年的生活，例如如何在社团、实习、成绩间取舍。2、毕业后从石油行业逐步过渡到金融行业，对如何转行，尤其是非金融学生如何找到一份适合自己的金融工作有深刻的认识，并能根据学生情况给出具体可实施的计划、找到适合学生的岗位并对如何准备面试等具体事项提供帮助。3、因为从事股权投资行业，所以对当下热门的行业都有所了解，例如互联网、人工智能、半导体、先进制造等，对各行业未来的趋势看的相对清楚，结合自己多年的留学经历与海外工作经历，如果你对选学校选专业有困惑，以及对自身在现有行业内的发展路径不清晰，都可以帮你更好的做出决定。目前的服务状态是不合作
编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang怎么样？编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7060.html；简介：拿到了香港城市大学（语言研究-翻译研究）/香港科技大学（中国文化）/比利时鲁汶大学(KU Leuven)（语言学高级硕士）/莱顿大学（语言学研究型硕士）/兰卡斯特大学（传播学）的offerIELTS （7.5），GPA: 3.3/4.0本身读的是汉语国际教育/英语，所以对语言学、应用语言学（对外汉语/对外汉语）、东亚语言文学、传播学、教育学有较多的了解现在在比利时的鲁汶，鲁汶是一个典型的欧洲大学城，几乎一半人口都是学生。目前的课程基本是深入的以研究为基础的，每一门课程都要求自己开展独立研究项目作为期末考核标准。上课人数是小班教学，每门课的人数在2-6个学生，因此在上课的时候能够和教授进行积极的互动。虽然是文科，我们还可以选定自己感兴趣的研究小组，联系老师，进研究小组进行相关的课题研究。目前的服务状态是可以受理

编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan怎么样？编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7055.html；简介：本科就读新加坡南洋理工大学电子与电机工程系，并以一等荣誉学位毕业；毕业后任职于世界500强企业，也是世界上最大的油田服务公司斯伦贝谢，从事项目管理相关工作；工作过程中想转行从事金融相关工作，就着手做了两件事，第一件事报考CFA，并在2018年通过三级考试并顺利持证；第二件事是申请金融相关的研究生，因为在海外时间比较长了，对申请学校也比较了解，所以是通过DIY的方式拿到了帝国理工（IC）、伦敦政经（LSE）以及伦敦大学学院（UCL）的offer并最终选择去帝国理工就读矿产与能源金融专业；研究生毕业后，经过一年的思考并了解各类金融相关工作，最终决定加入投资行业，并选择股权投资母基金这一细分领域，且很有幸的加入盈嘉资本担任投资经理一职。能为大家提供的帮助：1、在大学期间长期担任学生社团的管理层角色，且保持了相对高的成绩，对大学生活规划有独到的见解，可以帮助学生在入校之时就规划好大学四年的生活，例如如何在社团、实习、成绩间取舍。2、毕业后从石油行业逐步过渡到金融行业，对如何转行，尤其是非金融学生如何找到一份适合自己的金融工作有深刻的认识，并能根据学生情况给出具体可实施的计划、找到适合学生的岗位并对如何准备面试等具体事项提供帮助。3、因为从事股权投资行业，所以对当下热门的行业都有所了解，例如互联网、人工智能、半导体、先进制造等，对各行业未来的趋势看的相对清楚，结合自己多年的留学经历与海外工作经历，如果你对选学校选专业有困惑，以及对自身在现有行业内的发展路径不清晰，都可以帮你更好的做出决定。目前的服务状态是不合作
编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang怎么样？编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7060.html；简介：拿到了香港城市大学（语言研究-翻译研究）/香港科技大学（中国文化）/比利时鲁汶大学(KU Leuven)（语言学高级硕士）/莱顿大学（语言学研究型硕士）/兰卡斯特大学（传播学）的offerIELTS （7.5），GPA: 3.3/4.0本身读的是汉语国际教育/英语，所以对语言学、应用语言学（对外汉语/对外汉语）、东亚语言文学、传播学、教育学有较多的了解现在在比利时的鲁汶，鲁汶是一个典型的欧洲大学城，几乎一半人口都是学生。目前的课程基本是深入的以研究为基础的，每一门课程都要求自己开展独立研究项目作为期末考核标准。上课人数是小班教学，每门课的人数在2-6个学生，因此在上课的时候能够和教授进行积极的互动。虽然是文科，我们还可以选定自己感兴趣的研究小组，联系老师，进研究小组进行相关的课题研究。目前的服务状态是可以受理

编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan怎么样？编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7055.html；简介：本科就读新加坡南洋理工大学电子与电机工程系，并以一等荣誉学位毕业；毕业后任职于世界500强企业，也是世界上最大的油田服务公司斯伦贝谢，从事项目管理相关工作；工作过程中想转行从事金融相关工作，就着手做了两件事，第一件事报考CFA，并在2018年通过三级考试并顺利持证；第二件事是申请金融相关的研究生，因为在海外时间比较长了，对申请学校也比较了解，所以是通过DIY的方式拿到了帝国理工（IC）、伦敦政经（LSE）以及伦敦大学学院（UCL）的offer并最终选择去帝国理工就读矿产与能源金融专业；研究生毕业后，经过一年的思考并了解各类金融相关工作，最终决定加入投资行业，并选择股权投资母基金这一细分领域，且很有幸的加入盈嘉资本担任投资经理一职。能为大家提供的帮助：1、在大学期间长期担任学生社团的管理层角色，且保持了相对高的成绩，对大学生活规划有独到的见解，可以帮助学生在入校之时就规划好大学四年的生活，例如如何在社团、实习、成绩间取舍。2、毕业后从石油行业逐步过渡到金融行业，对如何转行，尤其是非金融学生如何找到一份适合自己的金融工作有深刻的认识，并能根据学生情况给出具体可实施的计划、找到适合学生的岗位并对如何准备面试等具体事项提供帮助。3、因为从事股权投资行业，所以对当下热门的行业都有所了解，例如互联网、人工智能、半导体、先进制造等，对各行业未来的趋势看的相对清楚，结合自己多年的留学经历与海外工作经历，如果你对选学校选专业有困惑，以及对自身在现有行业内的发展路径不清晰，都可以帮你更好的做出决定。目前的服务状态是不合作

编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang怎么样？编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7060.html；简介：拿到了香港城市大学（语言研究-翻译研究）/香港科技大学（中国文化）/比利时鲁汶大学(KU Leuven)（语言学高级硕士）/莱顿大学（语言学研究型硕士）/兰卡斯特大学（传播学）的offerIELTS （7.5），GPA: 3.3/4.0本身读的是汉语国际教育/英语，所以对语言学、应用语言学（对外汉语/对外汉语）、东亚语言文学、传播学、教育学有较多的了解现在在比利时的鲁汶，鲁汶是一个典型的欧洲大学城，几乎一半人口都是学生。目前的课程基本是深入的以研究为基础的，每一门课程都要求自己开展独立研究项目作为期末考核标准。上课人数是小班教学，每门课的人数在2-6个学生，因此在上课的时候能够和教授进行积极的互动。虽然是文科，我们还可以选定自己感兴趣的研究小组，联系老师，进研究小组进行相关的课题研究。目前的服务状态是可以受理

编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao怎么样？编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7061.html；简介：在香港一年多的时间，顺利完成学业，交友广泛，可以为学员分享香港tips和推荐稳定靠谱的房源！目前在国内top5综甲设计院工作～学长很爱交朋友，沉迷于音乐，本科时曾组建乐队，担任主音吉他手。日常会泡健身房，偶尔踢足球，喜欢旅行和摄影～学长从大四上拿了offer后，一直在做留学兼职，已成功帮多名学弟学妹拿到offer。非常熟悉香港，新加坡和英国的工科和商科专业的招生标准，申请流程，擅长为学生进行时间规划、择校和文书写作。除此之外，还可以指导学员进行背景提升、分享实习和求职经验。学员与我的关系不仅仅是服务和被服务，而是成为彼此相互信任的好友，学员入学后，在生活、学习、找实习、找工作时遇到问题都会找我咨询，我会用自己的经验和资源为学员指明方向～目前的服务状态是可以受理

编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang怎么样？编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7060.html；简介：拿到了香港城市大学（语言研究-翻译研究）/香港科技大学（中国文化）/比利时鲁汶大学(KU Leuven)（语言学高级硕士）/莱顿大学（语言学研究型硕士）/兰卡斯特大学（传播学）的offerIELTS （7.5），GPA: 3.3/4.0本身读的是汉语国际教育/英语，所以对语言学、应用语言学（对外汉语/对外汉语）、东亚语言文学、传播学、教育学有较多的了解现在在比利时的鲁汶，鲁汶是一个典型的欧洲大学城，几乎一半人口都是学生。目前的课程基本是深入的以研究为基础的，每一门课程都要求自己开展独立研究项目作为期末考核标准。上课人数是小班教学，每门课的人数在2-6个学生，因此在上课的时候能够和教授进行积极的互动。虽然是文科，我们还可以选定自己感兴趣的研究小组，联系老师，进研究小组进行相关的课题研究。目前的服务状态是可以受理
编号为235的申请导师Xuecong Li 怎么样？编号为235的申请导师Xuecong Li 官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7054.html；简介：-目前的服务状态是不合作
编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan怎么样？编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7055.html；简介：本科就读新加坡南洋理工大学电子与电机工程系，并以一等荣誉学位毕业；毕业后任职于世界500强企业，也是世界上最大的油田服务公司斯伦贝谢，从事项目管理相关工作；工作过程中想转行从事金融相关工作，就着手做了两件事，第一件事报考CFA，并在2018年通过三级考试并顺利持证；第二件事是申请金融相关的研究生，因为在海外时间比较长了，对申请学校也比较了解，所以是通过DIY的方式拿到了帝国理工（IC）、伦敦政经（LSE）以及伦敦大学学院（UCL）的offer并最终选择去帝国理工就读矿产与能源金融专业；研究生毕业后，经过一年的思考并了解各类金融相关工作，最终决定加入投资行业，并选择股权投资母基金这一细分领域，且很有幸的加入盈嘉资本担任投资经理一职。能为大家提供的帮助：1、在大学期间长期担任学生社团的管理层角色，且保持了相对高的成绩，对大学生活规划有独到的见解，可以帮助学生在入校之时就规划好大学四年的生活，例如如何在社团、实习、成绩间取舍。2、毕业后从石油行业逐步过渡到金融行业，对如何转行，尤其是非金融学生如何找到一份适合自己的金融工作有深刻的认识，并能根据学生情况给出具体可实施的计划、找到适合学生的岗位并对如何准备面试等具体事项提供帮助。3、因为从事股权投资行业，所以对当下热门的行业都有所了解，例如互联网、人工智能、半导体、先进制造等，对各行业未来的趋势看的相对清楚，结合自己多年的留学经历与海外工作经历，如果你对选学校选专业有困惑，以及对自身在现有行业内的发展路径不清晰，都可以帮你更好的做出决定。目前的服务状态是不合作
编号为1105的申请导师Yvonne Xu的教育经历是什么？就读学校：香港大学、就读专业金融学、学位理学硕士| Master of Science|MSc，入学日期、毕业日期，均分，GPA分，，学业状态，该学位是否为目前最高学历：否。

编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang怎么样？编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7060.html；简介：拿到了香港城市大学（语言研究-翻译研究）/香港科技大学（中国文化）/比利时鲁汶大学(KU Leuven)（语言学高级硕士）/莱顿大学（语言学研究型硕士）/兰卡斯特大学（传播学）的offerIELTS （7.5），GPA: 3.3/4.0本身读的是汉语国际教育/英语，所以对语言学、应用语言学（对外汉语/对外汉语）、东亚语言文学、传播学、教育学有较多的了解现在在比利时的鲁汶，鲁汶是一个典型的欧洲大学城，几乎一半人口都是学生。目前的课程基本是深入的以研究为基础的，每一门课程都要求自己开展独立研究项目作为期末考核标准。上课人数是小班教学，每门课的人数在2-6个学生，因此在上课的时候能够和教授进行积极的互动。虽然是文科，我们还可以选定自己感兴趣的研究小组，联系老师，进研究小组进行相关的课题研究。目前的服务状态是可以受理
编号为235的申请导师Xuecong Li 怎么样？编号为235的申请导师Xuecong Li 官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7054.html；简介：-目前的服务状态是不合作
编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao怎么样？编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7061.html；简介：在香港一年多的时间，顺利完成学业，交友广泛，可以为学员分享香港tips和推荐稳定靠谱的房源！目前在国内top5综甲设计院工作～学长很爱交朋友，沉迷于音乐，本科时曾组建乐队，担任主音吉他手。日常会泡健身房，偶尔踢足球，喜欢旅行和摄影～学长从大四上拿了offer后，一直在做留学兼职，已成功帮多名学弟学妹拿到offer。非常熟悉香港，新加坡和英国的工科和商科专业的招生标准，申请流程，擅长为学生进行时间规划、择校和文书写作。除此之外，还可以指导学员进行背景提升、分享实习和求职经验。学员与我的关系不仅仅是服务和被服务，而是成为彼此相互信任的好友，学员入学后，在生活、学习、找实习、找工作时遇到问题都会找我咨询，我会用自己的经验和资源为学员指明方向～目前的服务状态是可以受理

编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang怎么样？编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7060.html；简介：拿到了香港城市大学（语言研究-翻译研究）/香港科技大学（中国文化）/比利时鲁汶大学(KU Leuven)（语言学高级硕士）/莱顿大学（语言学研究型硕士）/兰卡斯特大学（传播学）的offerIELTS （7.5），GPA: 3.3/4.0本身读的是汉语国际教育/英语，所以对语言学、应用语言学（对外汉语/对外汉语）、东亚语言文学、传播学、教育学有较多的了解现在在比利时的鲁汶，鲁汶是一个典型的欧洲大学城，几乎一半人口都是学生。目前的课程基本是深入的以研究为基础的，每一门课程都要求自己开展独立研究项目作为期末考核标准。上课人数是小班教学，每门课的人数在2-6个学生，因此在上课的时候能够和教授进行积极的互动。虽然是文科，我们还可以选定自己感兴趣的研究小组，联系老师，进研究小组进行相关的课题研究。目前的服务状态是可以受理

编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao怎么样？编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7061.html；简介：在香港一年多的时间，顺利完成学业，交友广泛，可以为学员分享香港tips和推荐稳定靠谱的房源！目前在国内top5综甲设计院工作～学长很爱交朋友，沉迷于音乐，本科时曾组建乐队，担任主音吉他手。日常会泡健身房，偶尔踢足球，喜欢旅行和摄影～学长从大四上拿了offer后，一直在做留学兼职，已成功帮多名学弟学妹拿到offer。非常熟悉香港，新加坡和英国的工科和商科专业的招生标准，申请流程，擅长为学生进行时间规划、择校和文书写作。除此之外，还可以指导学员进行背景提升、分享实习和求职经验。学员与我的关系不仅仅是服务和被服务，而是成为彼此相互信任的好友，学员入学后，在生活、学习、找实习、找工作时遇到问题都会找我咨询，我会用自己的经验和资源为学员指明方向～目前的服务状态是可以受理
编号为234的申请导师Sheila Zhu怎么样？编号为234的申请导师Sheila Zhu官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7062.html；简介：目前的服务状态是不合作
编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan怎么样？编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7055.html；简介：本科就读新加坡南洋理工大学电子与电机工程系，并以一等荣誉学位毕业；毕业后任职于世界500强企业，也是世界上最大的油田服务公司斯伦贝谢，从事项目管理相关工作；工作过程中想转行从事金融相关工作，就着手做了两件事，第一件事报考CFA，并在2018年通过三级考试并顺利持证；第二件事是申请金融相关的研究生，因为在海外时间比较长了，对申请学校也比较了解，所以是通过DIY的方式拿到了帝国理工（IC）、伦敦政经（LSE）以及伦敦大学学院（UCL）的offer并最终选择去帝国理工就读矿产与能源金融专业；研究生毕业后，经过一年的思考并了解各类金融相关工作，最终决定加入投资行业，并选择股权投资母基金这一细分领域，且很有幸的加入盈嘉资本担任投资经理一职。能为大家提供的帮助：1、在大学期间长期担任学生社团的管理层角色，且保持了相对高的成绩，对大学生活规划有独到的见解，可以帮助学生在入校之时就规划好大学四年的生活，例如如何在社团、实习、成绩间取舍。2、毕业后从石油行业逐步过渡到金融行业，对如何转行，尤其是非金融学生如何找到一份适合自己的金融工作有深刻的认识，并能根据学生情况给出具体可实施的计划、找到适合学生的岗位并对如何准备面试等具体事项提供帮助。3、因为从事股权投资行业，所以对当下热门的行业都有所了解，例如互联网、人工智能、半导体、先进制造等，对各行业未来的趋势看的相对清楚，结合自己多年的留学经历与海外工作经历，如果你对选学校选专业有困惑，以及对自身在现有行业内的发展路径不清晰，都可以帮你更好的做出决定。目前的服务状态是不合作

编号为235的申请导师Xuecong Li 怎么样？编号为235的申请导师Xuecong Li 官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7054.html；简介：-目前的服务状态是不合作
编号为234的申请导师Sheila Zhu怎么样？编号为234的申请导师Sheila Zhu官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7062.html；简介：目前的服务状态是不合作
编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan怎么样？编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7055.html；简介：本科就读新加坡南洋理工大学电子与电机工程系，并以一等荣誉学位毕业；毕业后任职于世界500强企业，也是世界上最大的油田服务公司斯伦贝谢，从事项目管理相关工作；工作过程中想转行从事金融相关工作，就着手做了两件事，第一件事报考CFA，并在2018年通过三级考试并顺利持证；第二件事是申请金融相关的研究生，因为在海外时间比较长了，对申请学校也比较了解，所以是通过DIY的方式拿到了帝国理工（IC）、伦敦政经（LSE）以及伦敦大学学院（UCL）的offer并最终选择去帝国理工就读矿产与能源金融专业；研究生毕业后，经过一年的思考并了解各类金融相关工作，最终决定加入投资行业，并选择股权投资母基金这一细分领域，且很有幸的加入盈嘉资本担任投资经理一职。能为大家提供的帮助：1、在大学期间长期担任学生社团的管理层角色，且保持了相对高的成绩，对大学生活规划有独到的见解，可以帮助学生在入校之时就规划好大学四年的生活，例如如何在社团、实习、成绩间取舍。2、毕业后从石油行业逐步过渡到金融行业，对如何转行，尤其是非金融学生如何找到一份适合自己的金融工作有深刻的认识，并能根据学生情况给出具体可实施的计划、找到适合学生的岗位并对如何准备面试等具体事项提供帮助。3、因为从事股权投资行业，所以对当下热门的行业都有所了解，例如互联网、人工智能、半导体、先进制造等，对各行业未来的趋势看的相对清楚，结合自己多年的留学经历与海外工作经历，如果你对选学校选专业有困惑，以及对自身在现有行业内的发展路径不清晰，都可以帮你更好的做出决定。目前的服务状态是不合作

编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang怎么样？编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7060.html；简介：拿到了香港城市大学（语言研究-翻译研究）/香港科技大学（中国文化）/比利时鲁汶大学(KU Leuven)（语言学高级硕士）/莱顿大学（语言学研究型硕士）/兰卡斯特大学（传播学）的offerIELTS （7.5），GPA: 3.3/4.0本身读的是汉语国际教育/英语，所以对语言学、应用语言学（对外汉语/对外汉语）、东亚语言文学、传播学、教育学有较多的了解现在在比利时的鲁汶，鲁汶是一个典型的欧洲大学城，几乎一半人口都是学生。目前的课程基本是深入的以研究为基础的，每一门课程都要求自己开展独立研究项目作为期末考核标准。上课人数是小班教学，每门课的人数在2-6个学生，因此在上课的时候能够和教授进行积极的互动。虽然是文科，我们还可以选定自己感兴趣的研究小组，联系老师，进研究小组进行相关的课题研究。目前的服务状态是可以受理
编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan怎么样？编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7055.html；简介：本科就读新加坡南洋理工大学电子与电机工程系，并以一等荣誉学位毕业；毕业后任职于世界500强企业，也是世界上最大的油田服务公司斯伦贝谢，从事项目管理相关工作；工作过程中想转行从事金融相关工作，就着手做了两件事，第一件事报考CFA，并在2018年通过三级考试并顺利持证；第二件事是申请金融相关的研究生，因为在海外时间比较长了，对申请学校也比较了解，所以是通过DIY的方式拿到了帝国理工（IC）、伦敦政经（LSE）以及伦敦大学学院（UCL）的offer并最终选择去帝国理工就读矿产与能源金融专业；研究生毕业后，经过一年的思考并了解各类金融相关工作，最终决定加入投资行业，并选择股权投资母基金这一细分领域，且很有幸的加入盈嘉资本担任投资经理一职。能为大家提供的帮助：1、在大学期间长期担任学生社团的管理层角色，且保持了相对高的成绩，对大学生活规划有独到的见解，可以帮助学生在入校之时就规划好大学四年的生活，例如如何在社团、实习、成绩间取舍。2、毕业后从石油行业逐步过渡到金融行业，对如何转行，尤其是非金融学生如何找到一份适合自己的金融工作有深刻的认识，并能根据学生情况给出具体可实施的计划、找到适合学生的岗位并对如何准备面试等具体事项提供帮助。3、因为从事股权投资行业，所以对当下热门的行业都有所了解，例如互联网、人工智能、半导体、先进制造等，对各行业未来的趋势看的相对清楚，结合自己多年的留学经历与海外工作经历，如果你对选学校选专业有困惑，以及对自身在现有行业内的发展路径不清晰，都可以帮你更好的做出决定。目前的服务状态是不合作

编号为268的申请导师Tiffani S.的教育经历是什么？就读学校：康考迪亚大学、就读专业幼儿和基础教育学、学位文学学士| Bachelor of Arts|B.A.，入学日期2010-09-01、毕业日期2014-08-31，均分，GPA分，，学业状态毕业，该学位是否为目前最高学历：否。
学员背景：1教育经历：至就读北京电影学院影视制片管理，均分，GPA/，申请留学时的学业阶段是，海Born in a family of musicians, I was introduced to various kinds of artistic creation and obsessed with cinema from an early age. The classic works that impressed in my mind have been encouraging me to find out the stories behind them. Consequently, I chose to study Digital Media Technology at Beijing Film Academy for my bachelor degree and decided to pursue my career as a filmmaker in the future.As a student of BFA, I have received both theoratical and technical courses about cinema, such as, Film Cultrue Studies, Audio-Visual Language, Introduction to Media Technology and Digital Cinema Technology, etc. These courses enhance my knowledge about film production. In my sophomore year, I directed and co-produced a short film, A Whistle. It was my first time to engage myself in full production process. Due to the lack of experiences, our crew encoutered some difficulties during the shooting; however, the production manager repsonded to these quickly that saved our crew from falling apart. From this experience, I realized that, in addition to creativity and technical skills, the role of a producer and his/her ability of management and coordiantion are very important to film production as well.In spite of academic trainning and shooting assignment, I always look for opportunities to put what I have learned into practice. For instance, my internship at Cloud Production provides me with a fresh perspective to film production in today’s circumstances. Cloud Production, developed by Alibaba Pictures, is a promising software that aimed at improving the industrialization level for film companies and producers in China. During my internship, I participated in post-production, external communication and publicity copywriting as a production assistant. To be more specific, I was supposed to contact the media companies and producers to promote our online production management software. Conversations with these professionals enable me to develop a deeper insight into the industrialized process of domestic media productions. As digital management is widely used in overseas production industry, I hope that I can promote digital management in China and bring it into Chinese film industry as a producer, which stimulates my enthusiasm to go for further systematical study.As far as I am aware of my career direction, I would like to receive further education from Hong Kong Baptist University. The postgraduate program, Producing for Films, Television and New Media involves full-process production courses that plays a leading role in advanced media education among Asia. Rather than technical skills and aesthetic theotries learned from my undergradute schooling, I expect to expand my knowledge into commercial aspects of filmmaking, like, financing, marketing, and content analysis so that the value of film culture can be better conveyed to the audience. Hong Kong's filmmakers made the film industry famous around the world. The classic films of Hong Kong have become a cultural label for the city. Nowadays, the cultural industry is booming in the Mainland and film co-production with Hong Kong is increasing. I am very interested in study film and media production from the perspective of Hong Kong’s successful experiences. Combining with the techniques and theories that I have obtained in BFA, I believe that this program could lay a solid foundation for my graduate study and prepare myself for pursuing a career as a film producer in the future.
学员背景：1教育经历：至就读华中科技大学土木工程，均分，GPA/，申请留学时的学业阶段是大三，海Having been immersed in a world defined by civil engineering and construction, I have seen the incredible things that can be achieved by a well-conceived and effectively executed engineering project. I am absolutely determined to make a positive contribution to the world through civil engineering; to achieve my considerable ambitions it is essential that I gain the very best engineering training available.I am continually searching for new opportunities to learn more about civil engineering. I am an active student member of the Institute of Civil Engineers, the conferences and talks of which I attend whenever possible. Doing so has placed me in the fortunate position of gaining insights into the profession from established civil engineers.To broad my horizon about civil engineering, I participated in an exchange experience to National University of Singapore. Having listened to the speak given by prof. Deyuan Liu, I realised that, as a civil engineer, we should have the ability to solve practical problems, civil engineers should not only have a good foundation in mathematics and mechanics, but also value and develop imagination, creativity, interpersonal skills. I also learnt that creative thinking is essential for design and research, and engineers should be able to deal with people from all walks of life. From case studies delivered by prof. Deyuan Liu, I learnt that Singapore has a relatively small land area and is now expanding its urban space through three main models: upward development (skyscrapers), use of underground space and reclamation. In the future, Singapore's urban development will become even greener and more intelligent. The fact that Singapore is almost immune to natural disasters such as typhoons, earthquakes and tsunamis will make its structural design even more imaginative and artistic. Through participation in such events and through my own studies, I have developed interests in many different aspects of civil engineering. For example, at present I am particularly fascinated by the area of the structural engineering. Learning more about this inspires me towards the possibility of being involved in the future in engineering projects in which the analysis and design of structure under loading is involved. Such challenges convince me that a career as a civil engineer would be highly rewarding.By undertaking an internship in Hunan Construction Engineering Group, I have gained an excellent understanding of the considerations made by civil engineers when working on complex projects. During my internship, I assisted the engineers at the project site to complete construction tasks, recorded daily construction progress, inspected the construction techniques, quality and safety of the site and reported the site conditions in a timely manner. Upon this experience, I found that there is a gap between the real construction and the knowledge I learnt at degree level. To solve this, I asked questions to the contractors in the field, searched for relevant standard specifications and learnt to apply them. Moreover, I learnt how to use some of the instruments on the construction site, such as the total station, and how to solve some practical situations.My career ambition is to become a structural engineer and become a chartered civil engineer. I strongly believe that my flair for science, combined with my enthusiasm for problem-solving and overcoming difficult challenges will allow me to excel in this course. I have confidence that engineering is a field where I can apply my skills best and fully realise my potential. The University of Bath has an excellent reputation in the UK for its academic excellence. The University of Bath has an excellent record of achievement in the construction and civil engineering industries, particularly in the field of innovative materials. I was involved in the Undergraduate Innovation Project as an undergraduate and my research topic was 'Finite Element Simulation Studies of Fibre Reinforced Cement Matrix Composites', so I have a keen interest in the field of engineering materials and this was a key reason for choosing the University of Bath.

学员背景：1教育经历：2017-09-01至2021-07-01就读 中南大学自动化工学学士| Having recognized the indescribable fascination in Business and Data Analytics (MScBDA) throughout my various relevant experiences such as research works, internship and academic curriculum, I decide to fully devote myself to an enhanced learning in it. Discovered from my internship, my desire to continuously enhance my learnings of data analytics leads to my application for MSc in Business and Data Analytics (MScBDA) in CityUniversity of Hong Kong.To diversify my experiences, I am always seizing the best and most of every single opportunity from my undergraduate study in B.Eng. of Automation at Central South University (CSU), China. IT-related fields have been identified as my top interest for which I have been developing a comprehensive understanding and solid foundation in many ways. For instance, I have been consciously and proactively advancing my Mathematics knowledge, programming and data processing skills from the provided courses, as well as my voluntary participation in Mathematical and Interdisciplinary Contest in Modeling (MCM/ICM). During the contest, I was leading a team of 3 members to study and construct various models and algorithms for problem-solving. We managed to self learn and utilize SPSS Statistics software with MATLAB for big data extraction and deep analysis of Amazon.com product reviews for 3 selected products. Thereafter, we constructed a mathematical model and leveraged on Natural Language Processing (NLP), to quantify product reviews and their attributes in order to predict sales based on the determining factors of the products. Our excellent work eventually won us the Meritorious Prize (top 8%) for the contest.In addition, I have been constantly motivated to gain exposures of IS from both the academic and industrial worlds. To acquire the relevant industrial experience, recently I took up an internship as an Information System Engineer at “Yonyou Network Technology”, a leading ERP provider with over 2 million enterprise users worldwide. My responsibility was to understand the ERP and its eco-systems first and then customize and implement the system as per user’s needs. The internship required me to proactively reach out to various experts to gain a better overall picture of the ERP system, conduct user research and communicate with clients to find out their business needs. Another challenge during the internship was to enhance the existing data synchronization between ERP DB and intermediate libraries. Data loss happened pretty often due to the “total synchronization approach” once a day, and after my research and trials, I proposed to implement a new approach of “incrementalsynchronization”, which significantly improved the performance by 80% and reduced the  data loss error. I also managed to collaborate with an accountant intern and equipped her with essential IT knowledge before we teamed up to implement various configurations and environments for our clients. The project outcome was very satisfying and it also deepened my interest in IS.With my constant mission to advance the world with technologies, such as empowering better information flow within various Information Systems, my next goal is to broaden my data analytics knowledge and skillsets in a systematic and academic approach. Out of a wide range of reputed universities and programmes, MScBDA offered by CityU has been identified as the most effective step to upgrade myself. I plan to enhance my learningsof DB from “Database Management Systems” and “Data Mining”. I also anticipate upgrading my Intelligence Applications knowledge and skillsets, as well as sharing my past experiences with my student peers for mutual learning in “Business Intelligence Applications” and “Blockchain Technology and Business Applications”. What excites me the most from the curriculum is that I could work closely with my academic mentor in the Dissertation Project for a deeper dive into research topics such as exploring for improved performance and largerscale BDA in commercial domain. In addition to learn cutting-edge technologies and practices from the curriculum, I also wish to contribute to a collaborative learning culture by sharing my insights, past experiences, as well as my cultural background to my student peers, as I believe sharing is the best learning.I desire for admission into MScBDA by NTU, which would be bound to shape my career and future brightly. With all sincerity, your favorable consideration of my application would be highly appreciated.
学员背景：1教育经历：至就读，均分，GPA3.56/4，申请留学时的学业阶段是大三，海外本科成绩It seems to be my “genetic” passion to choose translation as a lifelong career. I have retained a keen interest in British and American culture since I was a child. With my growth, I liked reading Chinese versions of foreign novels, listening to English songs, watching English movies, and so on. Thus, I decided to learn English well in order to have a deeper understanding of English culture. Translation, which functions as a “bridge” linking different cultures, enables excellent works written in English and advanced ideas from foreign countries be translated into Chinese, my mother tongue, thereby offering Chinese people admiring Western culture access to sharing hobbies with each other. This can contribute to introduce Chinese culture to the world.Dujiangyan, my hometown, is a world-famous tourist city in Sichuan Province. During a summer vacation in high school, I became good friends with Chris, a foreign teacher who came to China for the first time in the cram school. I took her and her friends to visit Qingcheng Mountain and a well-known local night market in Dujiangyan, introducing the city to them in English and acting as an interpreter when they were shopping. After the trip, Chris told me that everyone had a great time and she really fell in love with the city from that day on. I felt very proud to hear that and experienced a sense of achievement as a translator for the first time. Since then, my passion for studying translation has been ignited and to be a translator who spreads Chinese and foreign cultures has also been like a deep-rooted seed in my heart waiting for a thriving spring.Good news is that it did not take me much time to embrace the first spring breeze when I began my undergraduate journey at Macao Polytechnic Institute from August 2016. Having realized the importance of a solid foundation in translation, I have spent 3 years focusing on the study about Chinese-English Translation and Interpretation during which I have obtained a comprehensive picture about translation and its sub-disciplines like Consecutive Interpreting. Although such learning process is tough, which involves reading plenty of literature, memorizing theoretical knowledge and doing a great many exercises, my interest in translation has been growing and I have achieved a good GPA (3.56/4.0) as well. Therefore, I have decided to continue my study in this realm after undergraduate graduation.Besides, I have participated in Macao Polytechnic Institute (MPI) English Debate Team from2017 till the present. As the Vice-Captain, I am responsible for training new recruits, pushing the WeChat Subscription and communicating with coaches and players. Meanwhile, I have assisted the captain in organizing various activities, such as welcoming new arrivals yearly, a series of debate competitions, etc. As a team member, I have taken part in various debate contests in and off campus, such as MPI English Debating Competition, Hong Kong Debate Open, Gongdong Debating Competition, and have obtained some prizes and scholarships. The most difficult aspect of these British Parliamentary style debates is that there is only 15 minutes to prepare for each motion, which involves debaters’ a wealth of background knowledge about the topic. Additionally, debaters’ brains need to work very fast and they should express their own ideas in English immediately, which requires a good command of English skills. This experience improves my English proficiency, cultivate my English thinking efficiently, and equip me with a variety of knowledge, which play an essential role in my translation study.Apart from debate activities, the translation project of “The calabash children” which belongs to the course “General Translation” in my sophomore year also left a deep impression on me. During this project, I teamed another 2 classmates up and each of us should translate a text respectively. Next came the group discussion, modification and integration of the final translation. Finally, our group gave a presentation in class to describe the difficulties encountered in the process and how the group came up with such a translation. Since our teacher always stressed that the translation is better than the best, so we were asked to revise our own translation repeatedly. However, after two or more revisions, I have no idea about where to start at all. At this moment, the group members played a key role. We exchanged translations with each other, and wrote down the pros and cons for improvement. My groupmates put forward many useful suggestions from the perspective different from mine. It was the first long translation I conducted and the trickiest thing was translating some long English complex sentences clearly and coherently into Chinese because English is a hypotaxis language whose sentences consist of many clauses. Fortunately, with the teacher's explanation and the interaction with groupmates, I realized that it was not necessary to follow the structure of the original text in a regular way, but to use various translation skills flexibly to convey the same information and feelings to readers as much as possible. Moreover, “The calabash children” is an African fairy tale, so cultural factors should be taken into consideration in the translation, helping to transform the unique cultural images of Africa into similar cultural images of China. In a word, this experience became an internal driving force for me to get closer to the real veil of literature translation, a special field.This year, it is my honor to serve as a student helper of Macao International Environmental Co-operation Forum Exhibition and Macao International Trade and Investment Fair. My responsibility is to provide translation service for exhibitors and coordinate the communication between companies and customers. This practice is totally different from the usual classroom ones because on-site interpretation requires oral expression ability and good psychological quality, quick response and even a wide range of knowledge to deal with different types of translation tasks calmly.In terms of career development, I hope to be a professional translator and continue my PhD study in literature translation if possible. Translation would still be my lifelong pursuit while there appeared a need for me to update my current knowledge and skills as well as accumulate related practical experience in this field. Under such circumstances, your MA in Translation is surely the perfect choice for me. Not only does The Chinese University of Hong Kong enjoy world-wide reputation in the translation realm with a long history, but also it is located in a perfect place where Chinese and English cultures and languages meet. Therefore, I am convinced that such an environment would provide me a comprehensive understanding of similarities and differences between languages and their cultures. Most importantly, this program will arm me with both translation theories and practical skills. It also offers some pragmatic courses covering various topics and sectors (business, law, media, etc.) tailored to needs of various students. In summary, it will be very helpful in preparing me better for being a qualified and professional practitioner in translation.

My father is a doctor at home, which makes me pay great attention to the problems between doctors and patients. It is easy to heal a person’s body, but it is hard to heal a person’s heart. I want to be able to help others like my father. Therefore, as the president of the student union, I actively carried out charity activities during the student union, such as discussing how to treat disabled people and caring for left-behind children. When helping others, I not only feel very happy inside, but also can develop my critical thinking ability and improve my social skills. Furthermore, I can also learn new technologies to expand my range of knowledge.During my digital media undergraduate study, I began to realize my social responsibility. What is more important here is to encourage people to think positively through digital media. Thanks to instructor Shaoke Zhang’s valuable feedback, it has taught me how to learn through the ROI flow theory model framework to analyse the staged experience of the player's psychology, and how to improve the game’s mechanisms according to this experience to allow a viewer to feel better. After his courses, I entered the Tencent Game opening courses called Game Design and Development. In these courses, I worked with eight partners to create an independent game Wilderness Ferryman. With the development problem, I figured out how to use the solid lines to control triggering conditions, so we added the solid lines in Unity3D with particle interactive effects. On the other hand, during my internship in the Onmyoji Division in Netease Games (one of the most acclaimed Japanese mobile games released in 2016) and Xuanyuanjian Studio (one of the most popular Chinese style games of the early 20th century), I was exposed to the needs of users through voice interaction and realised that it has great potential in enhancing the new media. But these bits of knowledge are not enough. There is too much advanced knowledge to absorb, such as digital design, coding. These shortcomings have motivated me to learn more and adapt to the needs of the future digital media industry.The reason why I would like to apply University of Edinburgh is that Edn has a close relationship with the digital media industry. New media design programme structure involves exploring specific directions for digital design and mobile games. At the same time, some optional workshops offered by Edn are also of interest and hard work like entrepreneurship. The settings of these courses make up for the lack of knowledge of my culture and 3D design. Edn is a very powerful university in the research field of knowledge. I believe that applying myself to the field of digital media design would be an amazing opportunity to embark upon a career in a field I feel particularly passionate about.

学员背景：1教育经历：2016-09-01至2021-06-30就读匹兹堡大学心理学理学学士| The COVID-19 pandemic swept across all of us, destructing lives and derailing normal functioning of schools and companies. In the face of such adversity confronting all of us, my belief is firm that the future of education increasingly lies in harnessing the power of learning sciences to design environment that optimally blends online and in-person instruction, and in implementing evidence-based practices that meet the needs of individual learners, including in long-distance settings. Therefore, I feel eager and well prepared to apply to the MA program in Learning Sciences at Arizona State University. Born and raised in China, I spent some of my high school years and all of my college years in the United States. My international background provided me with unique lens to examine real-world issues in education. Growing up, I felt repressed by the educational system in China and therefore, one of my pressing goals following graduation from the program is to join the emerging force that seeks to use learning sciences and design thinking to transform the current landscape of education from one that focuses on churning out individuals deprived of pleasure for learning and creativity, into one that encourages individuals in identifying and following paths that suit their interests.My passion for a career in education was further fueled since my decision to switch major and studied Applied Developmental Psychology. Prior to this switch, I struggled with chemistry and found it very difficult to connect with or perform well in the courses that I took. As someone who cares deeply for issues in education and is eager to find solutions to help struggling students, I decided to study developmental psychology and later found it to be my true calling. To put theories into practice, I was recommended by one of my professors to work as an intern at WQED in Pittsburgh. One of the educational apps designed by the company, called PBS kids, utilized educational games to engage learners and to teach them crucial skills in life and school. At one time, I helped with Read Across America and my responsibility included finding and recommending books in areas such as social emotional wellness, mathematics, and science from PBS kids and other websites.During the fall semester of my senior year, I applied and was accepted to the research team led by Dr. Tinukwa Boulder at University of Pittsburgh. I was tasked with two research projects, with one focusing on reviewing and summarizing research literature related to teaching computer science and computational thinking skills to K-12 students, and the other focused on using tools such as Qualtrics to conduct survey on user experience of leading learning management systems such as Canvas. I was also in charge of co-managing the online teaching site SharePoint and of writing two to three blogs per month on instructional technology and teaching for the site. At the moment, I am working with a colleague to write up a blog discussing how to promote inclusive student participation for online and hybrid courses, with a special focus on racial and socio- economic equity.I am well equipped to apply to the Learning Sciences program at ASU. I was irresistibly drawn to this program as I echo deeply with the program's philosophy emphasizing learning that happens beyond the confines of schools. To close off, as traditional learning was disrupted by the pandemic, the need is dire for us to be innovative in designing evidence-based learning environments that support informal and formal learning, as well as face-to-face and online learning. I believe my aspirations will be widely embraced and carefully attended to at Arizona State University.

The development of AI is always on the basis of good software engineering skills. In return, the need of powerful and convenient tools for AI acts as a strong stimuli to push software engineering forward. Such a trend of fusion even prompts the research in the intersection, such as data-driven software design. Being involved in this wave, I, an undergraduate in software engineering, keep experiencing such a drastic change.My first perception of this change is from the internship in video game design. After finishing several intermediate level courses on software engineering, I started to look for opportunities to practice what I learned. Soon I found a summer internship program on video game design, and I chose to reproduce the classic video game Flappy Bird. I started to learn the basic knowledge of computer graphics, and implemented a ray tracing rendering algorithm based on Unix. I would like to follow this path and dive deeper into the world of data science and visual computation from such a program, and my solid foundations in software engineering will help me learn it better. It is unique not only because of a high reputation on both teaching and research, but also on its highly cross-disciplinary and practical atmosphere. Furthermore, TU/e is also unique because of its close ties to the industry. Such an unparalleled advantage provides students with opportunities to experience the real R&D scenarios in top corporations including Phillips, NXP and ASML. This fashion can largely broadenmy horizons, and allows for the real applications of the knowledge I learn from the data science courses. Second, the program I am applying for is with high qualities. The courses contain not only various technical contents in different sub-areas, including some emerging and promising fields like urban computation, geographic data mining, and process mining but also stress the importance of building real systems. This perfect combination can help me get a detailed but all-round understanding of data science from the perspectives of both theories and applications.This makes the program so fascinating, and I am deeply attracted by it. Last but not the least, the thesis project 1 will train me to become a critical thinker and a qualified junior researcher. Except for this topic, I would also like to explore the explainable and interactive AI based on image analysis, so another good choice is to work on image-based explainable recommender systems with Prof. Mykola Pechenizkiy. Thanks to the abundant resources and excellent teachers provided by my school, I have acquired a preliminary knowledge of chemistry and material. There, my excellent performance in major core courses, including chemistry experiments, helps me lay a solid foundation, which may play a critical role in my later study. And there are many intersections between chemical engineering and polymer material engineering, such as colloids and biomedical polymers, which means more advantages I have in relevant aspects.To enhance my technical skills and specialist knowledge, I attended the project “Research on Synthesis and Antibacterial Activity of Ag / TiO2, Chitosan / Ag”. This is an innovative project for college students, in which I used CS / AgNPs and Ag / TiO2 composite antibacterial agents with chitosan and silver nitrate as raw materials, and determined the most suitable process parameters bringing the optimum inhibitory effect. I characterized the morphology, particle size, and modification of the composite antibacterial agents by SEM, UV-Vis, TEM, etc. and finally measured the minimum inhibitory concentration by double dilution method. Many common material characterization and detection techniques are used in this project, which may become a stepping stone on my forward path.I also participated in two internships during my vacation, which help me know more about the manufacture of modified plastic and ceramics to some extent. I was mainly responsible for the configuration of formulation, sampling inspection and verification of process parameters. Although it is a shame that the length of time is limited so that I could only acquire fundamental knowledge, this experience gives the confirmation of my interest in chemistry. At the same time, these internships may bring me a better understanding of material process than the students majoring in chemistry.Besides learning relative knowledge of chemistry, I also acquire knowledge aboutfinancial analysis as well as translation by myself to expand my views and foster different thinking models. The professional qualification certificates issued by the Securities Association of China and the Ministry of Human Resources and Social Security of China are affirmations of my ability. These may help me resolve problems with multi-angles and show my brave to explore new fields as well as my willing to accept new challenges. At the same time, it is beneficial to strengthen my self-study ability. That is to say, I can quickly grasp the core of subjects independently. Even in the face of the pressure and new challenges, the high efficiency and passion for learning are never absent. So I think I can handle the courses brought by this program.With the increasingly fiercer competitions, a higher degree is becoming much necessary than before. In order to become more competitive and to enrich my expertise, a master’s degree is becoming more important. Staying true to the inceptive goal, it is suitable for me to choose this programme, because it provides many relative lessons referring to various aspects about chemistry and polymers, which are consistent with my undergraduate major. Following these curriculums, I can deepen my understanding of chemistry and improve myself further.Since the foundation in 1905, NUS has been committed to becoming the top university in the globe. 学员背景：2教育经历：2019-09-01至2020-11-01就读，均分，GPA3.67/4，\"Visual media have the power to define the past and construct the present. Our memories are not connate and real, while they originate from the representation of mass media we are involved.\" These note from the class Mass Media and Popular Culture in Korea when I was a first-year student at Peking University (PKU) have inspired me to explore the areas of digital media, and transnational cultural communication. Hence, in the following years of my undergraduate study in Hebrew Language and Literature, and International Relations, I have dedicated every aspect of mine to explore the various facets of international and intercultural communication via the function of media, and continue to pursue my master's degree in Global Communication at Chinese University of Hong Kong (CUHK).From September 2016, I had spent a year as an exchange student at the Hebrew University of Jerusalem, and through such experience, I acquired the change to think about how media coverage functions to construct the public perception towards the Other, and to solidify the stereotypes which further enlarge the cultural gap. This developed Mediterranean country impressed with its western lifestyle and straightforward interpersonal relationships. I experienced cultural shocks when communicating with friends from Israel in campus and immersing myself in social media platforms, and on the other hand, such exchange experience also stimulated my interests in intercultural communication as the diverse cultural conflicts and fusion operating in this country. Consequently, I began to investigate the role of culture and media: how culture works to shape people's mental landscape, how different cultures are mediated by digital media platforms, and correspondingly, in what ways does the connection between culture and media influence the international relations in a macro level.Followed by my exchange-student life in Jerusalem, I worked as an intern journalist for China Radio International. I led a project on how citizens in Israel think about the differences between Israel and China, and interviewed 50 Israeli. When Israeli interviewees gave harsh comments on the \"autocratic communism party\" and \"inhumane assembly line\" in China, I found the salient embodiment of media bias, which pushed me to probe what factors drive to generate such media bias in Israel including the tacit western ideological hegemony and the stereotype against the socialist and 'oriental' country. Moreover, in November 2016, I also talked with 23 Chinese living in Israel about their impression on Israel, and this coverage was shown on Channel 10 of Israel National Television. Indeed, it was challenging to interview such a large number of respondents, which was an intensive training for me to improve personal interview and communication skills. Simultaneously, such a practice also acted as an in-depth observation of intercultural communication. From August to September 2017, I was a summer intern in the New Media Department, Xinhua News Agency, Beijing. Through browsing both Xinhua News Database and English-language media such as BBC and CNN, I was responsible for selecting and rewriting news to be published on Chinese social media platforms. At the same time, I operated the Global Quickview column, which is designed to share daily news highlights worldwide on a daily basis. My internships have not only enhanced my knowledge in journalism and new media, but consolidate my interests in intercultural communication and media representations. When I was searching, selecting and rewriting global news, I found how my personal positionality worked in this process, which was also the representation of culture's functions. I, as the editor, chose the news according to its importance and readability for Chinese audiences; hence the selection standard was highly influenced by the cultural repertoire.As a consequence, such a refection motivated me to examine the culture in a transnational perspective. In September 2017, I started my double degree in International Relations at PKU, which served as a supplement for my interests in culture and media. In particular, courses such as Ethic Issues in WouldPolitics, World Religions and International Society and Studies of Comparative Politics facilitated me to gain an overview of the studies of political economy and globalisation from the view of politics and international relations. In the module of Introduction to Nation-Sates, I learned the modernism and its relation with the mainstream nationalist theories. As Benedict Anderson suggests, nations are imagined communities. Local languages are disseminated through the printing media including novels and newspaper, and hence established the imagined bond between individuals. In line with Hobsbawm's argument which conceptualises the nation as an invented tradition, I gained an overall understanding of the 'nation' as a modern term, as a tool of the dominant to implement social control, and as a compulsory regulation. In addition, when studying the course An Introduction of Film Studies, I have learned the ideological critique originated from Althusser. Mass media exemplified by films not only play crucial roles in reiterating the ideology, but also work to re/construct the collective memory for the public. The well-known Chinese feminist film critic deployed the classic American movie Forrest Gump to elaborate how the film uses the protagonist's narrative to fill the gap and heal the trauma in American society and contemporary history caused by wars, economic crisis and polarisation of wealth. I consciously chose modules from a wide range of disciplines such as literary studies, cultural studies, film studies, international relations, politics, communications, and sociology. In the final year, I participated in the course Intercultural Communication, and began to enter the cultural studies area. For the summative assessment, I drew on the film The Joy Luck Club direct by Wayne Wang in 1993 to analyse how the Chinese national image was constructed in a transnational perspective. Employing the textual analysis, I found the three strategies drew on in the film narrative: stigmatising the Chinese traditional culture from a colonial perspective, centring culture as the central conflict, and imagining the cultural fusion as the final solution. As the original argument in this essay, I was awarded 93/100, which ranked top 1% among my cohort.In August 2018, out of my interests in how culture is mediated via different social media platforms, I participated in Media Division of the 12th Asian Future Political Leaders Forum at Seoul National University, South Korea. As the representative of Peking University, I discussed with students from Shanghai, Tokyo, Seoul and Taipei regarding the media's history and development in East Asia, new media and technology, the influence of media domestically and transnationally, et cetera. I also delivered a presentation on media and political participation in East Asia. Using the #MeToo movement as an example, I analysed how social media function to facilitate the social movement, and bridge the public and the government. China, in particular witness how #Me too movement on various social media platforms including WeChat, and Weibo enter into the agenda of the public sphere. Due to the strict media censorship and castrated freedom of speech in China, after women voiced their sexual harassment experiences on social media, which triggered public appeal and criticism toward the government, policy-makers were prompted to take effective measures to suppress the public outrage via banning certain articles or blocking the users who raised their voices. Additionally, I conducted a comparative study between mainland China, Taiwan, South Korea and Japan concerning the different media regulation systems, values and beliefs, and correspondingly, different methods taken by the officials.My undergraduate academic training in Middle Eastern languages, International Politics, as well as a wide range of disciplines including optional modules in communications, film and cultural studies, have enabled me to observe the interactions and conflicts among individuals from various angles. I found myself enchanted by Israeli culture and affairs, as well as how people retain their cultural and religious traditions and respond to the media coverage from different communities. Thus, for the undergraduate thesis, I examined the national image building and political expression of Israel in the Eurovision Song Contest. This dissertation focuses on Israeli entries in the Eurovision Song Contest, and discusses the connotational meanings existed in the performance, the selection of songs, and lyrics with reference to the historical contexts from 1973 to 2019. I firstly categorised the three periods which represented the different strategies deployed by Israeli contestants and officials: from 1973 to 1987, when Israel conformed with the tides of world peace; from 1988 to 2000, when Israelicontestants frequently expressed political stance; and from 2001 to 2019, when attendees deliberately avoided controversial agendas. Then, this paper concluded that building a peaceful and flourishing national image is the primary purpose of Israel, and its self-positioning is an independent \"Jewish\" and \"democratic\" country.In September 2019, I started my postgraduate programme in Global Communication at CUHK, where provides me with a perfect choice to further integrate my previous knowledge during undergraduate study, and offer me rigorous theoretical training in media and communications studies with reference to practical cases. In the core module Globalisation and Communication, I further explored the interrelations between political economy and global communication, especially the critique towards the neoliberalism, media imperialism and the conceptualisation of digital labour. It was in this course, and I got to know Prof Daya Thussu and his renowned book International Communication: Continuity and Change, which has inspired me significantly such as how to form the balanced flow of information, how to raise the voice from the global South in a digital and globalisational era, and how to cultivate and expand the influence of counter-flows and alternative media. Also, in the modules Seminar in Communication Theories and Communication in Intercultural Settings, I further gained knowledge concerning intercultural communication and identity politics, which is different from international communication focusing on the macro-level socio-political and economic communication. For the group work of the communication theories, we drew upon ethnography of communication (EOM) to observe how the WhatsApp translation group TheM helps Chinese ethnic monitory women accomplish their certain goals. Through the research experience in both communication theories and Applied Communication Research courses, I have obtained an in-depth knowledge in qualitative research methods: pros and cons in terms of interview and ethnography, and the crucial reflexivity when conducting research. For the master's dissertation, I intend to study the media representations of Israel on Chinese video-sharing platform Bilibili to conceptualise and reframe the term 'media representation' in the context of Chinese contemporary social media, and explore how the distant Other is represented and negotiated with Chinese social-cultural development.Finally, it can be seen my keen interests in international and intercultural communication with reference to the various functions of social media from my undergraduate study in different subjects, internships in Chinese media industries and research experience during my postgraduate programme. Thus, as an essential step to pursue my career goal as a researcher in international cultural communication, I desire to continue my PhD study in the School of Communication at Hong Kong Baptist University (HKBU) under the supervision of Prof Daya Thussu. HKBU is world-renowned for its cutting edge research in media and communication studies, especially its traditional focus on international and intercultural communications, and situated-researches within East Asian socio-cultural contexts. My PhD project will examine the media representations of the other nations on Chinese digital media platforms to interrogate the term 'representation' and its complex but subtle relations with the Other. I believe my previous study and research experience, my personal skill sets, including independent and critical thinking capabilities, make me well prepared for the future PhD study in the subject of communication. Thus, I do hope you could consider my application favourably.
学员背景：1教育经历：至就读四川大学档案学，均分，GPA3.32/4，申请留学时的学业阶段是大四As an undergraduate at Sichuan University, I majored in Archival Science. Through this course of study, I learned to retrieve and extract data into meaningful information. In the process, I came to realize that information management has a huge impact on business performance. It can provide a company with strategic choice insight and predict customer trends and behaviors, which drives effective decision-making and increases business productivity. I’m fascinated by this area, and spare no efforts to delve into it. Moreover, current archival management is still based on paper filing and cannot take advantage of information technology for efficiency improvement. I believe the Library and Information Management program at your Faculty of Education will help me enhance my information management ability in archives industry.Through the study of clerical science, and scientific file management, I have mastered the methods of archival management. In the class of electronic document management, I led the team to complete the analysis electronic archives management of both China and the United States, and learn many advanced foreign file management methods. Our team published a paper titled Application of Electronic Archives Management in the Information Age. This experience enhanced my desire to go abroad for study. In the course of Archives Compilation, I independently completed the compilation for the modern industrial development archives of my hometown Tangshan. This project is among the top ones in the course. During this compilation, I went to Provincial Archives, and extracted more than 200 text files and precious photos from countless documents. Meanwhile, my interest in information management was further reinforced by taking courses such as Information Management System, Office Automation System, etc. To be more competitive, I chose to study database courses and passed the National Computer Database test (Level 2), which has a very low passing rate. Passing this test directly largely increases my confidence in learning information management. I also gained and enhanced more technical skills in the study of Information Retrieval and Information Management courses.My passion for archives industry started with my internship in Zhongnan-Zhidi – one of top 20 real estate companies in China, at the beginning of my junior year. As an archivist intern, I was tasked to work on compiling, identifying, and archiving for real estate projects. During this task, I noticed that for archival management, our company lacked professional archivists, and heavily relied on interns to do simple file compilation. It resulted in low efficiency and vital documents lost. The current archival management for our company also did not meet the national archival requirements. Noticing this issue turned into a great experience, because I got the opportunity to work alongside with our teammates to make improvements. As the leader of our intern team, I led them to formulate specifications for our company’s archivalmanagement, design document filing mechanism, and created relevant standards, which made the archival management process more rigorous. This internship helped me to see how information management can affect a company’s efficiency, and further confirmed my decision to devote myself to the study of library and information management. At present, archival management is underestimated in Chinese enterprise management, and has great potential for improvement. I hope to grasp the crux of it, and become the leader of domestic archival management in the future.In my undergraduate study, I had a comprehensive understanding of how to retrieve and label data with high efficiency by creating data models and warehouses based on business rules using Python and SQL. One meaningful class project experience involved solving an existing business problem in Information Management System class. We conducted an investigation into Yunfeng Archive Company, the largest archive outsourcing company in Chengdu, China. The investigation results showed that, the current archive outsourcing market had severe issues with lacking professional employees, lots of repetitive work, low efficiency, document security, etc. To better reduce labor costs and improve efficiency and security, we created an automated records management system with Python and SQL. The main function for our system is automated data classification. Manually filing documents can be expensive, and time-consuming. Once we imported documents into our system, the system could be trained to accurately identify document types, and classify documents automatically. It could process and organize both structure and unstructured documents with a high degree of accuracy. It could provide with integrity and long term access to vital documents. This experience has enhanced my analytical skills and problem-solving abilities.In my internship at Alibaba, I was tasked to work on data analysis for the sales volume of Taobao’s headphones. I cleaned and extracted keywords from raw data, and visualized the relationship between various factors with the sales volume of headphones. Based on the visualization, I figured out that there are four main factors which affected the sales volume of headphones in Taobao: location, brand, price period, and credibility. Most customers had preferences for nearby warehouses for shipping, well-known brands, price period suitable for their salaries, and stores with high credibility. In order to give more satisfying customized service, I proposed and designed a recommendation system with my team members by using Amazon Machine Learning service. This system could figure out users’ buying preferences by analyzing headphones’ high sales volume and frequency, and increase the push of such headphones. This internship experience reinforced my strong technical and analytical skills, which will all be great assets for my future study.As the president of Colorful Stone, a public volunteer organization at Sichuan University sponsored by Chinese government, I honed my leadership abilities. After Wenchuan earthquake happened in 2008, we found one big part of rebuilding after Wenchuan earthquake was psychological counseling. In order to provide better support for children in those disaster areas, we founded this organization to give psychological guidance to them. During my chairman term, we expanded our connected schools from 8 to 13, and recruited more than 2,000 volunteers. After brainstorming with my officers, we set up training sessions with different themes for these children. To build a larger network and enhance communication, we arranged events connecting children from those disaster areas to student volunteers from both Sichuan University and Hong Kong Polytechnic University. I was also responsible for data management, optimization for redundant data, and training my officers about how to fully utilize the skills of Excel to manage large number of volunteer information data. I feel very self-satisfied and pleased during this volunteer experience.Currently, although archival management is underestimated, I realize it is very important in enterprises operation. The quality of archival management will directly affect administrative efficiency and utilization of document values. I believe your Library and Information Management program can broaden my horizons and enhance my information processing capabilities in archives industry. I hope I could better solve issues in archival management, and accelerate the development and progress of archives industry in the future.
