学员背景：1教育经历：至就读哈尔滨工业大学英语文学学士| Bachelor of Arts|B.My education dream starts with the initial inspiration my grandmother gave to me when I was a little girl. To help me write a composition named “An unforgettable day”, she took me outdoors for a picnic, sharing a beautiful day with me. At that time, I not only felt surprised about how smoothly I could complete my writing, but also inspired by this kind of teaching and educating that derived from practice. Once by chance, I become an English teacher of a left-behind boy. His parents entrusted him to my care, including his English language learning. I realised the duty I shouldered as a teacher, both in helping him improve his English language ability, as well as in imparting him effective English learning methods. Because of the poor economic conditions of his family, he had no access to standard English, let alone to learn it. In that case, I tried to use various teaching and learning approaches such as contextualised learning by using authentic English videos, and task-based learning by giving him some activities. Two years later, I was pleasantly surprised see him show up at the gate of my university and felt super honoured that I can give him a hand in his English learning journey as a teacher.As Albert Einstein said, what sculpture is to a block of marble, education is to a human soul. As for me, owing to the continuing respects and passions toward education, to be a responsible English teacher who teaches students knowledge, helps them pave their way for further education and gives them directions like lighthouses is always my dream. In my mind, University of Cambridge is one of the most influential universities in the world, and I am dearly keen on its great fame, precise spirit and picturesque surroundings. Concerning MPhil in Second Language Education, it is an excellent and attractive programme that aims to develop substantial knowledge and skills in researching language education, laying a solid foundation for full-scale PhD research.I studied English at Harbin Institute of Technology (HIT) from 2013-2017. Courses of this major are not restricted to involving theories that are related to English language, linguistics and translation, providing me with many insights in sociolinguistics, sociocultural theory and second language acquisition from language learners' perspective. Some courses like Intercultural Communication has indeed contributed to my understanding of the importance of culture and communication in acquiring a second language as well as adapting ourselves to this globalised and informalised world. Course named Translation and Interpreting (Chinese-English), which I obtained No.1 with 93.7/100 and 92/100 in my class has enhanced my pragmatic competence and strengthened my transferrable skills between L1 and L2. In general, no matter whether the course was about theories or practices, I have done a great job in my academics, receiving an average score of 85.6/100. Given my achievement in study, I was awarded two scholarships and a full CSC scholarship for the exchange programme to the University of New South Wales in Australia, which can demonstrate my strong ability in academic studies.My practical experience in education began with an internship in Pattison English when I was an undergraduate student. I enjoyed the time spending with my students to share my knowledge and release my passion. This internship provided me with an excellent opportunity to understand the real work of education by using various pedagogical approaches like role-playing, extensive reading, task-based learning, etc., stimulating me to know the great significance of learner’s motivation inlanguage learning. After graduation, I worked in English First (EF) as a full-time English teacher, teaching adult EFL learners English speaking. Compared with teenagers, adults have more intrinsic language learning motivation but are with poorer English language abilities. Due to the Critical Period Hypothesis I have learnt in class, I knew it is quite challengeable for them to correct some linguistic errors, let alone to reach a native-like level. Thus, assisting them to overcome the learning difficulties and guiding them to cultivate effective language learning strategies have become my predominant responsibilities. All in all, my working experience on education strengthened my dream in this field, but at the meantime, the gap between theories and practice now seems to be an obstacle in my way of future development. Therefore, I am more determined than ever to apply this programme at your university.Apart from academic study, my other interests also trained me into a comprehensibly capable student. I am fond of debating and have attended North China Debate Open in my 4th year. This competition made me familiarise with the British parliamentary system as well as the historical and brilliant culture of this country, increasingly benefiting me to acquire lots of communicative and debating skills. Fortunately, I was awarded the second prize in the end. As a minister of the International Communication Association of HIT, I welcomed and received the officers from Purdue University, responsible for scheduling their itinerary, arranging accommodation for them, translating and guiding them to visit in Harbin. Spending time with them, I gradually know how to express myself clearly, communicate with others appropriately, and tackle the difficulties effectively.Due to my outstanding performance, I was selected as an exchange student to visit the University of New South Wales in Australia with a full CSC scholarship. The exchange programme made me more familiar with the educating system in the western countries, which is entirely different from that in China. Also, it improved my English proficiency and expanded my vision to understand the diverse culture, making me more eager to study abroad and become a global citizen in the future.All the words are to show my great passion in this programme of your university. Benefiting from the well-organised courses from the Durham University together with the research experience under professional supervision, I am hoping that I can seize the opportunity after graduation to start my career as a teacher or researcher in English language education, making demanding contributions towards both the theoretical and practical aspects. I am pretty fascinated by the advanced facilities, world-class academics as well as friendly teachers and students in Cambridge. I do believe the master study there will be a memorable and essential experience in both my academic career and my life.
学员背景：1教育经历：2006-09-01至2010-06-30就读北京科技大学天津学院国际经济Essay 1 My best leadership experience as the general manager of WH International Casting LLC is to lead a diversified team of 12 high-potential managers and team members from China and the US to achieve its business model transformation during the US-China trade conflict. Over the past 3 years, the tariff has forced more of our clients to source outside China. I was concerned about the 55% loss of topline in 2019, which could wipe out all profits from 2016 to 2018, and even worse, would put my company out of business and my employees out of jobs. After experiencing suffered toss and twists and conducting thorough market research, I took significant interventions to transform the company from a traditional manufacturing-driven business model into a more profitable and flexible supply chain service-driven model, as it is an indispensable part of global business no matter where the clients purchase. The first task for me was to define the company’s new 5-year strategy and develop comprehensive business cases for both shareholders, who got skeptical that a business model change would make things better at their course. I delivered 10+ presentations mainly from inevitable industry direction impacted by the trade conflict, short/mid/long-term financial outlooks from more strategic revenue management, and the industry’s growing demands for high-quality supply chain services.Indeed, the transformation could not be achieved on my own. After getting the top management’s alignments, I turned to the individuals who had the right skills and styles for that job. I noticed that some of my managers and team members were a bit lost facing such abrupt changes and challenges. I also brought in OKR (Objectives andKey Results) system to ensure my team well aware of our shared vision and mission, yearly/quarterly/monthly priorities, and their contributions were visible to all team members, so they got greatly encouraged and became more proactive in working out creative ideas and plans to achieve goals. Moreover, despite the challenges of the company’s finances, I invested 10% of annual profits to employee training of all levels, featured with supply chain management, BI application, and lean management, so that they could pick up any skill they need to develop or upgrade.The transformation finally turned out to a significant breakthrough with two VMI projects launched, successfully turning around the business by growing its gross margin from 15% to 35% and generating sustainable cash flow starting from Mar.2020, which effectively responded to the tariff and the unexpected COVID-19 pandemic, and both shareholders are completely convinced. Moreover, the learning culture cultivated through this experience enables all team members always to think differently and creatively. I feel more confident to continue to drive changes and lead the company to the next level.Essay 2Being the General Manager of WH International Casting LLC for five years, I have formed my short-term goal to bring it to the next level, achieving triple-digit year-on-year topline growth to $30M. Secondly, I have rich work experience across different functions with multinational companies, enabling myself to manage diverse teams in different environments, which is an added skill coming in handy during the EMBA study. Finally, I have a vivid life experience by traveling and living in more than 20 countries. I believe wisdom comes with life experience, and I am fully prepared to embrace all the new opportunities in the EMBA program.After talking with my friend May Wang, a second-year student of Anderson EMBA, I am excited to learn ‘Think Fearlessly and Drive Change’ is embedded deeply in Anderson’s culture. 学员背景：1教育经历：至就读上海师范大学计算机科学与技术理学学士| Bachelor DegreI always thought the vast majority of my life but didn’t have a clear goal until a piece of news caught my eyes one day: A company called Datago applied Machine Learning and NLP techniques to financial statements. With passion for programming, I led College Student Innovation and Entrepreneurship Training Program at third year in university where I set up a makeup service named Queen by means of Augmented Reality technology. My novel idea for AR lipstick fitting helped me got municipal project approval which was rare in our college. After getting the approval, we conducted surveys on the operating habits of consumers in the form of online questionnaires. We found that consumers were more likely to accept the operation forms like single-finger movement and two-finger zoom. So, we determined the two operation steps of identification and calculation after brainstorming according to the survey result. We encountered difficulty that the actual zoom range of the picture didn’t match the range of finger movement. To solve this problem, I discussed with my team members firstly and then browsed literatures that provided some inspirations to us. Putting these methods into practice we solved the problem at certain level. Then we consulted the instructor and professional teachers. Under the guidance of teachers, we optimized the algorithm for calculating the zoom range into three steps: get the center point of the gestures, use point.set (x/2, y/2) to set the touch point and calculate distance by Math.sqrt(Math.pow(x, 2) + Math.pow(y, 2)), which solved the problem of inaccurate zoom range calculation. When coming to detailed implementation problems, such as pan distance and rotation range calculation, I tried to find a way to improve the accuracy of recognition for pan distance, rotation range through reading papers. After analysing the functions of the MotionEvent package, I adjusted the super parameters like number of iterations to enhance its recognition accuracy. Due to my unremitting effort, the accuracy of the function jumped from 78% to 93%.Never feeling content the achievements I made, I realized that my bottleneck lay in the lack of profound and comprehensive about real work practices. With my rich research experience, I received offers from Wingtech Technology Co., Ltd. (listing company, largest ODM company in the world and largest semiconductor company in China) and Accenture (Fortune Global 500, acceptance rate: 5%) at the same time. After consideration, I chose to join Wingtech Technology Co., Ltd. as a Camera effect engineer for its more attractive capacity development plan. My role was to debug the shooting effect of the mobile phone camera which includes brightness, color, offset noise points, etc. and independently responsible for AE project and improved the Histogram algorithm using C. The biggest challenge I faced was the optimization of Histogram algorithm, which meant I had to be familiar with the construction and execution of the original algorithm and found where can be improved in a quite short project period. As a self-driven person, I set a series of clear objectives about reading source code and papers. After several end-late workdays, I found the relationships between internal small modules and how they affect each other’s work, which led to a main reason of poor brightness effect. Then, I tried to adjust the parameters of each small modules separately to compare and improve the original one. Without a doubt, I received good feedback from customers and an A in performance appraisal. The valuable working experience exercised my debugging, problem-solving and leadership ability. My professional abilities are used more efficiently in practice, and have been rapidly improved in an environment of fierce competition.My primary goal is to prepare myself for a Data Scientist career and persist in lifelong research in the future. 学员背景：1教育经历：至就读中国海洋大学国际经济与贸易经济学学士| Bachelor of EcOver the past few years, the international collaboration has been facing great challenges. The global political environment was reshaped by events like US denying the NAFTA, Briexit, and Sino-Hong Kong conflicts. That news stimulated my interest in the international relations and the problems embedded in the current global economy. As a result, my curiosity has brought me to the front door of the Master of International Studies at the City University of Hong Kong.Majoring in International Economics and Trade at the Ocean University of China enabled me the ability to identify economic forces shaping the international policies. The curriculum structure of the program not only provided me with plenty of economic models but also developed comprehensive logical thinking and problem-solving skills. Business courses such as Microeconomics, Macroeconomics, International Finance, and Accounting have established my thorough understanding of the national economy and business operations. Meanwhile, learning Econometrics, Probabilities, and Statistics, has laid a solid technical foundation to develop the trending data analytics skills for my postgraduate study. Moreover, achieving outstanding student in 2016 would also evidence my endeavors to strive for academic excellence, and I will continue my upward trend to excel in your program.With the passion for international studies, I have seized every opportunity to conduct theory-based analyses. I began my research journey with a project to discover the innovative hypotheses between China’s land sales and credit measures: How did the banks credit inflates the land sales? I collected data from WIND database on land sales, money supply, bank loans, wealth management products, and bond and equity issuance, and then used Excel for OLS regression and hypothesis test to analyze whether bank loans are major driving forces of China’s land sales. Eventually, I got the result that while bank loans have significant results in pushing up the housing prices in tier 1 and 2 cities, real estates in other cities are mostly financed by shadow banking products. And my comparative analysis between the 2007 U.S. subprime mortgage crisis and China’s current mortgage conditions indicated a great crisis embedded in China’s shadow banking sectors. This comprehensive project has allowed me to gain a taste of academic research, at the same time made me fell fulfilling for its important regional policy implications.Craving more empirical research on governance challenges, I actively engaged in the Student Research Development Program at Ocean University of China (OUC-SRDP), where I find empirical evidences linking the real estate property prices and bank credits. After retrieving real estate prices, GDP per capita, average salary, population, and interest rate of 35 cities from 2003 to 2015 from the CEInet Industry and Statistics Databases and National Bureau of Statistics, I analyzed the mingled effects of household incomes, interest rate changes, and bank credits using fixed effect models and random effect models in STATA. Controlled for GDP, save, wage, and population, we found significant positive relationships between bank interest rates and the housing prices. 1% increase in the 6 months interest rate would lead to 0.102% increase in housing prices, while the long-terminterest rates have significant but smaller impacts to the housing prices. This finding is counterintuitive, but we do find a fanaticism effect of the buyers in China’s real state market. My superior was impressed to see my ability to finish a research project and provide macro policy recommendations to echo the real estate bubbles in China.On top of macro topics, I was also eager to nurture my analytical skills through performing sound empirical methodologies. For instance, I completed an econometrics project investigating the determining factors of China’s film box office earnings out of interests. Realizing the dynamic development in the Chinese film market, I would like to contribute to the previous literature by incorporating recent years updates. With no structured data, I manually collected the data from box office revenue from ChinaBoxOffice.com, audience ratings from douban.com, and row piece-rate from maoyan.com supplemented with web search. Then I ran multiple OLS regressions and robustness tests such as G-Q tests, White tests, and heteroscedastic correction with 57 movie samples in EViews. As a result, I concluded that audience ratings, filming costs, and piece-rates have significant positive correlations with the box office revenue of a film. Realizing the possibility to explore unlimited fields, I further confirmed my goal to be a professional academic researcher.Apart from academic exploration, I also engaged in extracurricular activities to enhance my communication skills and inform my academic interests. I participated in an international volunteer program to teach local kids Chinese in Bali, Indonesia. My experiences with the underprivileged students motivated me to develop professionalism in international development economics to uncover the reason for poverty and wealth gaps. In addition, I took the responsibility of the news and information department head in the Ocean University Student Association. I formed a team with a group of five students to learn photographing, news editing, storytelling, as well as blogging through WeChat public accounts. This is a unique experience which cultivated my project management, teamwork, and fast learning skills that would contribute to my academic career in the future.Upon graduation, I am determined to pursue a peruse a Ph.D. in Economics. I firmly believe that the Master of International Studies program at CityU is exactly the right option for me. Since the program is the ONLY one of its kind in Hong Kong that develops expertise on issues of Asian and International Studies, it will allow me to gain competitive advantages in research topics and develop interesting thesis. For instance, the course international political economy and East Asia and the US: Conflict and Interdependence would allow me to investigate in details international topics like most recent U.S. China Trade War. In addition, international relations in northeast Asia course meets my desire to gain more sophisticated undemanding in the trending political challenges of China. Moreover, the valuable opportunities to attend academic conferences, undertake a field studies all around Asia, and achieve publications fascinates me. Finally, after consulting International Studies alumni, I am convinced that CityU’s numerous research resources, various ways of teaching methods, and a potential of academic publications, will facilitate my career pursuits in Academia.The International Studies curriculum at CityU is the best preparation for me to develop advanced skills in academic research, problem-solving and economic analysis. I have enough confidence to believe that I would become an ambitious, energetic, and determined Ph.D. student after graduating from the International Studies program. Ultimately, I am genuinely passionate about the unsolved problem of the wealth gap and cultural topics. I would, therefore, relish the opportunity to study international studies at the truly prestigious CityU faculty.
学员背景：1教育经历：2014-09-01至2018-06-01就读香港理工大学传达设计，均分，I define myself as an observer, a thinker and a maker. My interest in the GID program (London- Pratt-Keio track) stems from the program’s inclusive design methodologies, its emphasis on social innovation, and its value on community.First, I’m interested to practice more about the inclusive design methodologies that had been applied in thousands of projects in RCA.Last year, I worked as Student Assistant with HHCD Researcher Gabriele Meldailyte at PolyU to research and design for the silver-aged in Hong Kong, focusing on ‘technology + elderly’, and was introduced ‘inclusive design’. At RCA, I would like to explore more about inclusive design through social innovation projects. I cared about today's most pressing social challenges like aging society, I’m particularly committed to designing for the Age 2.0 generations to motivate lasting change and societal impact during my master’s studies. I believe innovation is about looking ahead, and that GID will help me create impactful designs. Through connections to professors and the cohort in industrial design, business and mechanical engineering and by acquiring new skills in developing sustainable business models and production feasibility, such as applying image processing and IoT technologies, I seek to create innovative products-service systems for the future. I believe that the RCA community is made up of excellent people of diverse backgrounds, and I wish to be one of them. Since good design comes from intense activity and interactions, my cohort will be an important learning resource and problem-solving asset.My ultimate goal after graduation is to become a design strategist, like GID alumni , able to impact people’s lives by using design thinking at a strategic level, as a creative catalyst, designing innovation-led solutions for social change. With my connections to local startups and incubators, my secondary goal is to found an agency to provide customized design consultancy services to tech-based startups by integrating design thinking and strategies into their initial stages which will create impactful and profitable products in a global context.To achieve these goals, I’d like to utilize the complementary expertise and resources of six leading institutions based in five international centres of design to accumulate professional design experience. I also look forward to experiencing different roles in the research and development process, such as product manager, user researcher, and other business functions during course projects in order to practice my skills in problem identification, analysis and decision-making.I’m thoroughly prepared to join RCA. Integrating my knowledge in user-centered design through course works and internships, I practiced ethnographic design research methodologies while honing my rapid prototyping skills in delivering design outcomes. I’m passionate about exploring how the implementation of new technologies can leverage the overall user experience of digital products. In building the OptiCare app for diagnosing eye tiredness, prototyping Fido (an IoT pet toy), and creating the HOWRU platform as a co-founder, I have realized the greater power of design + technology. Taking a further step into the computer science field, I taught myself Python for Research, Swift, and building hybrid web apps.I was inspired about the future of human-centered design from my voluntary experience at the International Experience Design Conference in Beijing this past June. The idea of ‘data-enabled design’ as a tool to ‘optimize, differentiate, and innovate’ powerfully pointed out how human- centered design can empower people through active design possibilities for building a more sustainable future. Thus, it is my dream to make an impact with design towards the sustainable development of both human life and the environments in which we live. I am looking forward to joining the M.A. GID program to make my dreams come real!
学员背景：1教育经历：至就读中国海洋大学国际经济与贸易经济学学士| Bachelor of EcOver the past few years, the international collaboration has been facing great challenges. The global political environment was reshaped by events like US denying the NAFTA, Briexit, and Sino-Hong Kong conflicts. That news stimulated my interest in the international relations and the problems embedded in the current global economy. As a result, my curiosity has brought me to the front door of the Master of International Studies at the City University of Hong Kong.Majoring in International Economics and Trade at the Ocean University of China enabled me the ability to identify economic forces shaping the international policies. The curriculum structure of the program not only provided me with plenty of economic models but also developed comprehensive logical thinking and problem-solving skills. Business courses such as Microeconomics, Macroeconomics, International Finance, and Accounting have established my thorough understanding of the national economy and business operations. Meanwhile, learning Econometrics, Probabilities, and Statistics, has laid a solid technical foundation to develop the trending data analytics skills for my postgraduate study. Moreover, achieving outstanding student in 2016 would also evidence my endeavors to strive for academic excellence, and I will continue my upward trend to excel in your program.With the passion for international studies, I have seized every opportunity to conduct theory-based analyses. I began my research journey with a project to discover the innovative hypotheses between China’s land sales and credit measures: How did the banks credit inflates the land sales? I collected data from WIND database on land sales, money supply, bank loans, wealth management products, and bond and equity issuance, and then used Excel for OLS regression and hypothesis test to analyze whether bank loans are major driving forces of China’s land sales. Eventually, I got the result that while bank loans have significant results in pushing up the housing prices in tier 1 and 2 cities, real estates in other cities are mostly financed by shadow banking products. And my comparative analysis between the 2007 U.S. subprime mortgage crisis and China’s current mortgage conditions indicated a great crisis embedded in China’s shadow banking sectors. This comprehensive project has allowed me to gain a taste of academic research, at the same time made me fell fulfilling for its important regional policy implications.Craving more empirical research on governance challenges, I actively engaged in the Student Research Development Program at Ocean University of China (OUC-SRDP), where I find empirical evidences linking the real estate property prices and bank credits. After retrieving real estate prices, GDP per capita, average salary, population, and interest rate of 35 cities from 2003 to 2015 from the CEInet Industry and Statistics Databases and National Bureau of Statistics, I analyzed the mingled effects of household incomes, interest rate changes, and bank credits using fixed effect models and random effect models in STATA. Controlled for GDP, save, wage, and population, we found significant positive relationships between bank interest rates and the housing prices. 1% increase in the 6 months interest rate would lead to 0.102% increase in housing prices, while the long-terminterest rates have significant but smaller impacts to the housing prices. This finding is counterintuitive, but we do find a fanaticism effect of the buyers in China’s real state market. My superior was impressed to see my ability to finish a research project and provide macro policy recommendations to echo the real estate bubbles in China.On top of macro topics, I was also eager to nurture my analytical skills through performing sound empirical methodologies. For instance, I completed an econometrics project investigating the determining factors of China’s film box office earnings out of interests. Realizing the dynamic development in the Chinese film market, I would like to contribute to the previous literature by incorporating recent years updates. With no structured data, I manually collected the data from box office revenue from ChinaBoxOffice.com, audience ratings from douban.com, and row piece-rate from maoyan.com supplemented with web search. Then I ran multiple OLS regressions and robustness tests such as G-Q tests, White tests, and heteroscedastic correction with 57 movie samples in EViews. As a result, I concluded that audience ratings, filming costs, and piece-rates have significant positive correlations with the box office revenue of a film. Realizing the possibility to explore unlimited fields, I further confirmed my goal to be a professional academic researcher.Apart from academic exploration, I also engaged in extracurricular activities to enhance my communication skills and inform my academic interests. I participated in an international volunteer program to teach local kids Chinese in Bali, Indonesia. My experiences with the underprivileged students motivated me to develop professionalism in international development economics to uncover the reason for poverty and wealth gaps. In addition, I took the responsibility of the news and information department head in the Ocean University Student Association. I formed a team with a group of five students to learn photographing, news editing, storytelling, as well as blogging through WeChat public accounts. This is a unique experience which cultivated my project management, teamwork, and fast learning skills that would contribute to my academic career in the future.Upon graduation, I am determined to pursue a peruse a Ph.D. in Economics. I firmly believe that the Master of International Studies program at CityU is exactly the right option for me. Since the program is the ONLY one of its kind in Hong Kong that develops expertise on issues of Asian and International Studies, it will allow me to gain competitive advantages in research topics and develop interesting thesis. For instance, the course international political economy and East Asia and the US: Conflict and Interdependence would allow me to investigate in details international topics like most recent U.S. China Trade War. In addition, international relations in northeast Asia course meets my desire to gain more sophisticated undemanding in the trending political challenges of China. Moreover, the valuable opportunities to attend academic conferences, undertake a field studies all around Asia, and achieve publications fascinates me. Finally, after consulting International Studies alumni, I am convinced that CityU’s numerous research resources, various ways of teaching methods, and a potential of academic publications, will facilitate my career pursuits in Academia.The International Studies curriculum at CityU is the best preparation for me to develop advanced skills in academic research, problem-solving and economic analysis. I have enough confidence to believe that I would become an ambitious, energetic, and determined Ph.D. student after graduating from the International Studies program. Ultimately, I am genuinely passionate about the unsolved problem of the wealth gap and cultural topics. I would, therefore, relish the opportunity to study international studies at the truly prestigious CityU faculty.

编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan怎么样？编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7055.html；简介：本科就读新加坡南洋理工大学电子与电机工程系，并以一等荣誉学位毕业；毕业后任职于世界500强企业，也是世界上最大的油田服务公司斯伦贝谢，从事项目管理相关工作；工作过程中想转行从事金融相关工作，就着手做了两件事，第一件事报考CFA，并在2018年通过三级考试并顺利持证；第二件事是申请金融相关的研究生，因为在海外时间比较长了，对申请学校也比较了解，所以是通过DIY的方式拿到了帝国理工（IC）、伦敦政经（LSE）以及伦敦大学学院（UCL）的offer并最终选择去帝国理工就读矿产与能源金融专业；研究生毕业后，经过一年的思考并了解各类金融相关工作，最终决定加入投资行业，并选择股权投资母基金这一细分领域，且很有幸的加入盈嘉资本担任投资经理一职。能为大家提供的帮助：1、在大学期间长期担任学生社团的管理层角色，且保持了相对高的成绩，对大学生活规划有独到的见解，可以帮助学生在入校之时就规划好大学四年的生活，例如如何在社团、实习、成绩间取舍。2、毕业后从石油行业逐步过渡到金融行业，对如何转行，尤其是非金融学生如何找到一份适合自己的金融工作有深刻的认识，并能根据学生情况给出具体可实施的计划、找到适合学生的岗位并对如何准备面试等具体事项提供帮助。3、因为从事股权投资行业，所以对当下热门的行业都有所了解，例如互联网、人工智能、半导体、先进制造等，对各行业未来的趋势看的相对清楚，结合自己多年的留学经历与海外工作经历，如果你对选学校选专业有困惑，以及对自身在现有行业内的发展路径不清晰，都可以帮你更好的做出决定。目前的服务状态是不合作

编号为1105的申请导师Yvonne Xu的教育经历是什么？就读学校：香港大学、就读专业金融学、学位理学硕士| Master of Science|MSc，入学日期、毕业日期，均分，GPA分，，学业状态，该学位是否为目前最高学历：否。
学员背景：1教育经历：至就读中央民族大学法学，均分，GPA3.47/5，申请留学时的学业阶段是，It has been 13 years since I witnessed my mom and her colleagues were doing compulsory demolition and removal on TV. They were moving expensive furniture out of the house of people who didn’t agree on the compensation conditions with clear shouts and cries around. While the officers worked well-organized and indifferently in the screen, the resident of the house was sitting on the ground outside the warning line, with his clothes ripped and torn, crying helplessly and angrily. I held confidence in the government’s acts and the law regulating their acts, until it was my grandparents’ turn to give way to new buildings planned by the government and deconstruct their home after 6 years. The government couldn’t reach to an indemnification agreement with people under its plan, including my family, as we were not willing to give up part of our rights. To my astonishment, my mom was threatened by her office leader of the demolition and relocation office if she continued to refused to cooperate with the government deconstruction plan. In the meantime, the window of my grandparents’ house was broken at midnight. The crying and shouting of the people who was forcibly resettled on television 6 years ago came to my mind while I was cleaning fragments of glass from the broken window. I know I need to do something for this situation. I checked the administrative regulations of our city in an effort of my family argue with the government office with nothing supportive, and even helpful, found. I know there must be something wrong. The law in this field confused me and I believed the power of government was obviously not restrained in a right way.Studying law is a way I can think of to solve my confusion and I became a law student five years ago. During my process of learning Administration Act Law and writing my graduate thesis, I found that there are many deficiencies in the legal procedure of compulsory demolition and removal, including the aspects of policy-making, execution and supervisory. After visiting the empty petition office hall where should have people come and appeal, it came to me that deficiencies not only exist in the policy itself, but also exist within the government system, about how power should be distributed and regulated between the higher and the lower level of governments.In preparation of the meeting on preferential policies the Asian Infrastructure Investment Bank, a multilateral development organization of an intergovernmental nature, can get after China became the host country, I conducted research about preferential policies for employees of different private companies, state-owned company, and non-profit organization from the aspects of different phases of employees’ career for the team. As I walked through my research results, to some degree, I found out that those preferential policies were factually power rent-seeking which abused social resources.There were deeper problem shown when I interned in the court. I was quite confused why there were few administrative lawsuits showed up. The most administrative cases I involved were non-litigation which only including coordinator procedure and directly making executive determinations. After extensive communication with the plaintiffs I met, they actually seldom realized they were able to encounter government through legal procedure in front of the judge to protect their own civil rights as they didn’t believe the local courts were truly independent from government power, and sadly, they were right.My childhood experience led me to figure out a right way to restrain government power. The college education I received showed me the deficiencies in our administrative system from various perspectives. My internship in law firm gave me a chance to glimpse part of the relationship among government power and civil rights while my court internship showed the current situation of what our judicial system can do. It is time for me to prepare myself to become an administrative litigation lawyer and do something for this situation in the future. After learning basic knowledge of relevant Chinese laws and regulations, it is a must for me to look at what the other country is doing. The constitutional legal system of the U.S. is one of the most comprehensive and perfect legal system in the modern world which impressed me from the initial stage of my law study, these famous constitutional rights campaigns for civil rights and stunning cases in the history reshape the power between citizens and governments, and the modern world as well. I believe Georgetown University can help me not only because of your great constitutional law professors, but also your prestigious reputation of international law. Courses like Comparative Constitutional Law will give me a chance to study on comparison in constitutional aspects, which can let me know more about the process of making constitution, power distribution of different legal subjects, the relationship between government power and judicial power, and civil rights protection and evolution. Additionally, GULC’s perfect location, where numbers of power sectors, international organizations are located and its ExternshipDatabase will provide me with plenty of opportunities to absorb knowledge from public sector, private sector and think-tank symposiums, like Harrison Institute of Public Law, where I can have a more direct understanding of how the US is governed and the interaction between American politics and law. I believe an education in Georgetown General Studies LL.M. will provide invaluable experiences and skills that can lead me to know more about the power of government and civil rights and become a professional lawyer in the field of constitutional and administrative law.

学员背景：1教育经历：至就读中国海洋大学国际经济与贸易经济学学士| Bachelor of EcTo Whom It May Concern:I am glad to write this recommendation for Miss Jiaxue Yu to study in your program. Jiaxue entered the School of Economics, Ocean University of China to study the Bachelor of Economics in International Economics and Trade in August 2015. As the dean of the faculty of international economics and trade and her lecturer in social investigation, international trade, and import and export practices courses, I have witnessed her growth over the past two years from a freshman to an active leader in the student association.Jiaxue impressed me with her leadership skills and her unwavering strive for excellence. As the head of the News and Information Department in the student association of the Ocean University of China, she has formed a team in organizing student activities and writing articles to promote the faculty. As her dean, I also noticed that she has been awarded by the faculty for several years for her academic excellence. Furthermore, Jiaxue has exhibited a strong motivation for the financial industry. I believe that Jiaxue has the capability to handle difficulties and achieve her plans.As Jiaxue’s lecturer, I find that she is scrupulous with academic research. In the early stage, she actively discussed the economics topics and research ideas with me. She took the initiative to read tremendous domestic and foreign literature, and finally selected an interesting topic assessing the impact of bank credits on China’s real estate prices in the undergraduate research project of the Ocean University. In her research, she applied multiple theories learned in my class to her study. For example, she leveraged the OLS methods in STATA to unveil the relationships between banks credit and housing prices, analyzed different credit measures such as interest rate, money supply, and shadow banking indicators, and conducted in-depth robustness tests and detailed comparative analysis before concluding her research. Her efforts and meticulous attitude have won her unanimous praise from the research committee as well as a good score for the course.In short, she is strict with herself in many aspects and has been constantly developing herself. After graduation, she chooses to set foot on the journey of studying in the Nanyang Technological University. I believe that your distinguished MSc in Applied Economics program matches perfectly with her future career goal of working in the financial industry. I sincerely hope that you can give her the opportunity for advanced study so that she can make better progress and contribute her talents to your esteemed university.Sincerely,Gao JintianProfessorDean, Faculty of International Economics and Trade, School of Economics,Ocean University of China
编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao怎么样？编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7061.html；简介：在香港一年多的时间，顺利完成学业，交友广泛，可以为学员分享香港tips和推荐稳定靠谱的房源！目前在国内top5综甲设计院工作～学长很爱交朋友，沉迷于音乐，本科时曾组建乐队，担任主音吉他手。日常会泡健身房，偶尔踢足球，喜欢旅行和摄影～学长从大四上拿了offer后，一直在做留学兼职，已成功帮多名学弟学妹拿到offer。非常熟悉香港，新加坡和英国的工科和商科专业的招生标准，申请流程，擅长为学生进行时间规划、择校和文书写作。除此之外，还可以指导学员进行背景提升、分享实习和求职经验。学员与我的关系不仅仅是服务和被服务，而是成为彼此相互信任的好友，学员入学后，在生活、学习、找实习、找工作时遇到问题都会找我咨询，我会用自己的经验和资源为学员指明方向～目前的服务状态是可以受理

编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang怎么样？编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7060.html；简介：拿到了香港城市大学（语言研究-翻译研究）/香港科技大学（中国文化）/比利时鲁汶大学(KU Leuven)（语言学高级硕士）/莱顿大学（语言学研究型硕士）/兰卡斯特大学（传播学）的offerIELTS （7.5），GPA: 3.3/4.0本身读的是汉语国际教育/英语，所以对语言学、应用语言学（对外汉语/对外汉语）、东亚语言文学、传播学、教育学有较多的了解现在在比利时的鲁汶，鲁汶是一个典型的欧洲大学城，几乎一半人口都是学生。目前的课程基本是深入的以研究为基础的，每一门课程都要求自己开展独立研究项目作为期末考核标准。上课人数是小班教学，每门课的人数在2-6个学生，因此在上课的时候能够和教授进行积极的互动。虽然是文科，我们还可以选定自己感兴趣的研究小组，联系老师，进研究小组进行相关的课题研究。目前的服务状态是可以受理
编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan怎么样？编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7055.html；简介：本科就读新加坡南洋理工大学电子与电机工程系，并以一等荣誉学位毕业；毕业后任职于世界500强企业，也是世界上最大的油田服务公司斯伦贝谢，从事项目管理相关工作；工作过程中想转行从事金融相关工作，就着手做了两件事，第一件事报考CFA，并在2018年通过三级考试并顺利持证；第二件事是申请金融相关的研究生，因为在海外时间比较长了，对申请学校也比较了解，所以是通过DIY的方式拿到了帝国理工（IC）、伦敦政经（LSE）以及伦敦大学学院（UCL）的offer并最终选择去帝国理工就读矿产与能源金融专业；研究生毕业后，经过一年的思考并了解各类金融相关工作，最终决定加入投资行业，并选择股权投资母基金这一细分领域，且很有幸的加入盈嘉资本担任投资经理一职。能为大家提供的帮助：1、在大学期间长期担任学生社团的管理层角色，且保持了相对高的成绩，对大学生活规划有独到的见解，可以帮助学生在入校之时就规划好大学四年的生活，例如如何在社团、实习、成绩间取舍。2、毕业后从石油行业逐步过渡到金融行业，对如何转行，尤其是非金融学生如何找到一份适合自己的金融工作有深刻的认识，并能根据学生情况给出具体可实施的计划、找到适合学生的岗位并对如何准备面试等具体事项提供帮助。3、因为从事股权投资行业，所以对当下热门的行业都有所了解，例如互联网、人工智能、半导体、先进制造等，对各行业未来的趋势看的相对清楚，结合自己多年的留学经历与海外工作经历，如果你对选学校选专业有困惑，以及对自身在现有行业内的发展路径不清晰，都可以帮你更好的做出决定。目前的服务状态是不合作

编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao怎么样？编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7061.html；简介：在香港一年多的时间，顺利完成学业，交友广泛，可以为学员分享香港tips和推荐稳定靠谱的房源！目前在国内top5综甲设计院工作～学长很爱交朋友，沉迷于音乐，本科时曾组建乐队，担任主音吉他手。日常会泡健身房，偶尔踢足球，喜欢旅行和摄影～学长从大四上拿了offer后，一直在做留学兼职，已成功帮多名学弟学妹拿到offer。非常熟悉香港，新加坡和英国的工科和商科专业的招生标准，申请流程，擅长为学生进行时间规划、择校和文书写作。除此之外，还可以指导学员进行背景提升、分享实习和求职经验。学员与我的关系不仅仅是服务和被服务，而是成为彼此相互信任的好友，学员入学后，在生活、学习、找实习、找工作时遇到问题都会找我咨询，我会用自己的经验和资源为学员指明方向～目前的服务状态是可以受理
编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan怎么样？编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7055.html；简介：本科就读新加坡南洋理工大学电子与电机工程系，并以一等荣誉学位毕业；毕业后任职于世界500强企业，也是世界上最大的油田服务公司斯伦贝谢，从事项目管理相关工作；工作过程中想转行从事金融相关工作，就着手做了两件事，第一件事报考CFA，并在2018年通过三级考试并顺利持证；第二件事是申请金融相关的研究生，因为在海外时间比较长了，对申请学校也比较了解，所以是通过DIY的方式拿到了帝国理工（IC）、伦敦政经（LSE）以及伦敦大学学院（UCL）的offer并最终选择去帝国理工就读矿产与能源金融专业；研究生毕业后，经过一年的思考并了解各类金融相关工作，最终决定加入投资行业，并选择股权投资母基金这一细分领域，且很有幸的加入盈嘉资本担任投资经理一职。能为大家提供的帮助：1、在大学期间长期担任学生社团的管理层角色，且保持了相对高的成绩，对大学生活规划有独到的见解，可以帮助学生在入校之时就规划好大学四年的生活，例如如何在社团、实习、成绩间取舍。2、毕业后从石油行业逐步过渡到金融行业，对如何转行，尤其是非金融学生如何找到一份适合自己的金融工作有深刻的认识，并能根据学生情况给出具体可实施的计划、找到适合学生的岗位并对如何准备面试等具体事项提供帮助。3、因为从事股权投资行业，所以对当下热门的行业都有所了解，例如互联网、人工智能、半导体、先进制造等，对各行业未来的趋势看的相对清楚，结合自己多年的留学经历与海外工作经历，如果你对选学校选专业有困惑，以及对自身在现有行业内的发展路径不清晰，都可以帮你更好的做出决定。目前的服务状态是不合作
编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang怎么样？编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7060.html；简介：拿到了香港城市大学（语言研究-翻译研究）/香港科技大学（中国文化）/比利时鲁汶大学(KU Leuven)（语言学高级硕士）/莱顿大学（语言学研究型硕士）/兰卡斯特大学（传播学）的offerIELTS （7.5），GPA: 3.3/4.0本身读的是汉语国际教育/英语，所以对语言学、应用语言学（对外汉语/对外汉语）、东亚语言文学、传播学、教育学有较多的了解现在在比利时的鲁汶，鲁汶是一个典型的欧洲大学城，几乎一半人口都是学生。目前的课程基本是深入的以研究为基础的，每一门课程都要求自己开展独立研究项目作为期末考核标准。上课人数是小班教学，每门课的人数在2-6个学生，因此在上课的时候能够和教授进行积极的互动。虽然是文科，我们还可以选定自己感兴趣的研究小组，联系老师，进研究小组进行相关的课题研究。目前的服务状态是可以受理

编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan怎么样？编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7055.html；简介：本科就读新加坡南洋理工大学电子与电机工程系，并以一等荣誉学位毕业；毕业后任职于世界500强企业，也是世界上最大的油田服务公司斯伦贝谢，从事项目管理相关工作；工作过程中想转行从事金融相关工作，就着手做了两件事，第一件事报考CFA，并在2018年通过三级考试并顺利持证；第二件事是申请金融相关的研究生，因为在海外时间比较长了，对申请学校也比较了解，所以是通过DIY的方式拿到了帝国理工（IC）、伦敦政经（LSE）以及伦敦大学学院（UCL）的offer并最终选择去帝国理工就读矿产与能源金融专业；研究生毕业后，经过一年的思考并了解各类金融相关工作，最终决定加入投资行业，并选择股权投资母基金这一细分领域，且很有幸的加入盈嘉资本担任投资经理一职。能为大家提供的帮助：1、在大学期间长期担任学生社团的管理层角色，且保持了相对高的成绩，对大学生活规划有独到的见解，可以帮助学生在入校之时就规划好大学四年的生活，例如如何在社团、实习、成绩间取舍。2、毕业后从石油行业逐步过渡到金融行业，对如何转行，尤其是非金融学生如何找到一份适合自己的金融工作有深刻的认识，并能根据学生情况给出具体可实施的计划、找到适合学生的岗位并对如何准备面试等具体事项提供帮助。3、因为从事股权投资行业，所以对当下热门的行业都有所了解，例如互联网、人工智能、半导体、先进制造等，对各行业未来的趋势看的相对清楚，结合自己多年的留学经历与海外工作经历，如果你对选学校选专业有困惑，以及对自身在现有行业内的发展路径不清晰，都可以帮你更好的做出决定。目前的服务状态是不合作
编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao怎么样？编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7061.html；简介：在香港一年多的时间，顺利完成学业，交友广泛，可以为学员分享香港tips和推荐稳定靠谱的房源！目前在国内top5综甲设计院工作～学长很爱交朋友，沉迷于音乐，本科时曾组建乐队，担任主音吉他手。日常会泡健身房，偶尔踢足球，喜欢旅行和摄影～学长从大四上拿了offer后，一直在做留学兼职，已成功帮多名学弟学妹拿到offer。非常熟悉香港，新加坡和英国的工科和商科专业的招生标准，申请流程，擅长为学生进行时间规划、择校和文书写作。除此之外，还可以指导学员进行背景提升、分享实习和求职经验。学员与我的关系不仅仅是服务和被服务，而是成为彼此相互信任的好友，学员入学后，在生活、学习、找实习、找工作时遇到问题都会找我咨询，我会用自己的经验和资源为学员指明方向～目前的服务状态是可以受理

编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang怎么样？编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7060.html；简介：拿到了香港城市大学（语言研究-翻译研究）/香港科技大学（中国文化）/比利时鲁汶大学(KU Leuven)（语言学高级硕士）/莱顿大学（语言学研究型硕士）/兰卡斯特大学（传播学）的offerIELTS （7.5），GPA: 3.3/4.0本身读的是汉语国际教育/英语，所以对语言学、应用语言学（对外汉语/对外汉语）、东亚语言文学、传播学、教育学有较多的了解现在在比利时的鲁汶，鲁汶是一个典型的欧洲大学城，几乎一半人口都是学生。目前的课程基本是深入的以研究为基础的，每一门课程都要求自己开展独立研究项目作为期末考核标准。上课人数是小班教学，每门课的人数在2-6个学生，因此在上课的时候能够和教授进行积极的互动。虽然是文科，我们还可以选定自己感兴趣的研究小组，联系老师，进研究小组进行相关的课题研究。目前的服务状态是可以受理

编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan怎么样？编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7055.html；简介：本科就读新加坡南洋理工大学电子与电机工程系，并以一等荣誉学位毕业；毕业后任职于世界500强企业，也是世界上最大的油田服务公司斯伦贝谢，从事项目管理相关工作；工作过程中想转行从事金融相关工作，就着手做了两件事，第一件事报考CFA，并在2018年通过三级考试并顺利持证；第二件事是申请金融相关的研究生，因为在海外时间比较长了，对申请学校也比较了解，所以是通过DIY的方式拿到了帝国理工（IC）、伦敦政经（LSE）以及伦敦大学学院（UCL）的offer并最终选择去帝国理工就读矿产与能源金融专业；研究生毕业后，经过一年的思考并了解各类金融相关工作，最终决定加入投资行业，并选择股权投资母基金这一细分领域，且很有幸的加入盈嘉资本担任投资经理一职。能为大家提供的帮助：1、在大学期间长期担任学生社团的管理层角色，且保持了相对高的成绩，对大学生活规划有独到的见解，可以帮助学生在入校之时就规划好大学四年的生活，例如如何在社团、实习、成绩间取舍。2、毕业后从石油行业逐步过渡到金融行业，对如何转行，尤其是非金融学生如何找到一份适合自己的金融工作有深刻的认识，并能根据学生情况给出具体可实施的计划、找到适合学生的岗位并对如何准备面试等具体事项提供帮助。3、因为从事股权投资行业，所以对当下热门的行业都有所了解，例如互联网、人工智能、半导体、先进制造等，对各行业未来的趋势看的相对清楚，结合自己多年的留学经历与海外工作经历，如果你对选学校选专业有困惑，以及对自身在现有行业内的发展路径不清晰，都可以帮你更好的做出决定。目前的服务状态是不合作
编号为234的申请导师Sheila Zhu怎么样？编号为234的申请导师Sheila Zhu官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7062.html；简介：目前的服务状态是不合作
编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang怎么样？编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7060.html；简介：拿到了香港城市大学（语言研究-翻译研究）/香港科技大学（中国文化）/比利时鲁汶大学(KU Leuven)（语言学高级硕士）/莱顿大学（语言学研究型硕士）/兰卡斯特大学（传播学）的offerIELTS （7.5），GPA: 3.3/4.0本身读的是汉语国际教育/英语，所以对语言学、应用语言学（对外汉语/对外汉语）、东亚语言文学、传播学、教育学有较多的了解现在在比利时的鲁汶，鲁汶是一个典型的欧洲大学城，几乎一半人口都是学生。目前的课程基本是深入的以研究为基础的，每一门课程都要求自己开展独立研究项目作为期末考核标准。上课人数是小班教学，每门课的人数在2-6个学生，因此在上课的时候能够和教授进行积极的互动。虽然是文科，我们还可以选定自己感兴趣的研究小组，联系老师，进研究小组进行相关的课题研究。目前的服务状态是可以受理

编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan怎么样？编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7055.html；简介：本科就读新加坡南洋理工大学电子与电机工程系，并以一等荣誉学位毕业；毕业后任职于世界500强企业，也是世界上最大的油田服务公司斯伦贝谢，从事项目管理相关工作；工作过程中想转行从事金融相关工作，就着手做了两件事，第一件事报考CFA，并在2018年通过三级考试并顺利持证；第二件事是申请金融相关的研究生，因为在海外时间比较长了，对申请学校也比较了解，所以是通过DIY的方式拿到了帝国理工（IC）、伦敦政经（LSE）以及伦敦大学学院（UCL）的offer并最终选择去帝国理工就读矿产与能源金融专业；研究生毕业后，经过一年的思考并了解各类金融相关工作，最终决定加入投资行业，并选择股权投资母基金这一细分领域，且很有幸的加入盈嘉资本担任投资经理一职。能为大家提供的帮助：1、在大学期间长期担任学生社团的管理层角色，且保持了相对高的成绩，对大学生活规划有独到的见解，可以帮助学生在入校之时就规划好大学四年的生活，例如如何在社团、实习、成绩间取舍。2、毕业后从石油行业逐步过渡到金融行业，对如何转行，尤其是非金融学生如何找到一份适合自己的金融工作有深刻的认识，并能根据学生情况给出具体可实施的计划、找到适合学生的岗位并对如何准备面试等具体事项提供帮助。3、因为从事股权投资行业，所以对当下热门的行业都有所了解，例如互联网、人工智能、半导体、先进制造等，对各行业未来的趋势看的相对清楚，结合自己多年的留学经历与海外工作经历，如果你对选学校选专业有困惑，以及对自身在现有行业内的发展路径不清晰，都可以帮你更好的做出决定。目前的服务状态是不合作

编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang怎么样？编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7060.html；简介：拿到了香港城市大学（语言研究-翻译研究）/香港科技大学（中国文化）/比利时鲁汶大学(KU Leuven)（语言学高级硕士）/莱顿大学（语言学研究型硕士）/兰卡斯特大学（传播学）的offerIELTS （7.5），GPA: 3.3/4.0本身读的是汉语国际教育/英语，所以对语言学、应用语言学（对外汉语/对外汉语）、东亚语言文学、传播学、教育学有较多的了解现在在比利时的鲁汶，鲁汶是一个典型的欧洲大学城，几乎一半人口都是学生。目前的课程基本是深入的以研究为基础的，每一门课程都要求自己开展独立研究项目作为期末考核标准。上课人数是小班教学，每门课的人数在2-6个学生，因此在上课的时候能够和教授进行积极的互动。虽然是文科，我们还可以选定自己感兴趣的研究小组，联系老师，进研究小组进行相关的课题研究。目前的服务状态是可以受理

编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan怎么样？编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7055.html；简介：本科就读新加坡南洋理工大学电子与电机工程系，并以一等荣誉学位毕业；毕业后任职于世界500强企业，也是世界上最大的油田服务公司斯伦贝谢，从事项目管理相关工作；工作过程中想转行从事金融相关工作，就着手做了两件事，第一件事报考CFA，并在2018年通过三级考试并顺利持证；第二件事是申请金融相关的研究生，因为在海外时间比较长了，对申请学校也比较了解，所以是通过DIY的方式拿到了帝国理工（IC）、伦敦政经（LSE）以及伦敦大学学院（UCL）的offer并最终选择去帝国理工就读矿产与能源金融专业；研究生毕业后，经过一年的思考并了解各类金融相关工作，最终决定加入投资行业，并选择股权投资母基金这一细分领域，且很有幸的加入盈嘉资本担任投资经理一职。能为大家提供的帮助：1、在大学期间长期担任学生社团的管理层角色，且保持了相对高的成绩，对大学生活规划有独到的见解，可以帮助学生在入校之时就规划好大学四年的生活，例如如何在社团、实习、成绩间取舍。2、毕业后从石油行业逐步过渡到金融行业，对如何转行，尤其是非金融学生如何找到一份适合自己的金融工作有深刻的认识，并能根据学生情况给出具体可实施的计划、找到适合学生的岗位并对如何准备面试等具体事项提供帮助。3、因为从事股权投资行业，所以对当下热门的行业都有所了解，例如互联网、人工智能、半导体、先进制造等，对各行业未来的趋势看的相对清楚，结合自己多年的留学经历与海外工作经历，如果你对选学校选专业有困惑，以及对自身在现有行业内的发展路径不清晰，都可以帮你更好的做出决定。目前的服务状态是不合作

编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang怎么样？编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7060.html；简介：拿到了香港城市大学（语言研究-翻译研究）/香港科技大学（中国文化）/比利时鲁汶大学(KU Leuven)（语言学高级硕士）/莱顿大学（语言学研究型硕士）/兰卡斯特大学（传播学）的offerIELTS （7.5），GPA: 3.3/4.0本身读的是汉语国际教育/英语，所以对语言学、应用语言学（对外汉语/对外汉语）、东亚语言文学、传播学、教育学有较多的了解现在在比利时的鲁汶，鲁汶是一个典型的欧洲大学城，几乎一半人口都是学生。目前的课程基本是深入的以研究为基础的，每一门课程都要求自己开展独立研究项目作为期末考核标准。上课人数是小班教学，每门课的人数在2-6个学生，因此在上课的时候能够和教授进行积极的互动。虽然是文科，我们还可以选定自己感兴趣的研究小组，联系老师，进研究小组进行相关的课题研究。目前的服务状态是可以受理
编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao怎么样？编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7061.html；简介：在香港一年多的时间，顺利完成学业，交友广泛，可以为学员分享香港tips和推荐稳定靠谱的房源！目前在国内top5综甲设计院工作～学长很爱交朋友，沉迷于音乐，本科时曾组建乐队，担任主音吉他手。日常会泡健身房，偶尔踢足球，喜欢旅行和摄影～学长从大四上拿了offer后，一直在做留学兼职，已成功帮多名学弟学妹拿到offer。非常熟悉香港，新加坡和英国的工科和商科专业的招生标准，申请流程，擅长为学生进行时间规划、择校和文书写作。除此之外，还可以指导学员进行背景提升、分享实习和求职经验。学员与我的关系不仅仅是服务和被服务，而是成为彼此相互信任的好友，学员入学后，在生活、学习、找实习、找工作时遇到问题都会找我咨询，我会用自己的经验和资源为学员指明方向～目前的服务状态是可以受理

编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang怎么样？编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7060.html；简介：拿到了香港城市大学（语言研究-翻译研究）/香港科技大学（中国文化）/比利时鲁汶大学(KU Leuven)（语言学高级硕士）/莱顿大学（语言学研究型硕士）/兰卡斯特大学（传播学）的offerIELTS （7.5），GPA: 3.3/4.0本身读的是汉语国际教育/英语，所以对语言学、应用语言学（对外汉语/对外汉语）、东亚语言文学、传播学、教育学有较多的了解现在在比利时的鲁汶，鲁汶是一个典型的欧洲大学城，几乎一半人口都是学生。目前的课程基本是深入的以研究为基础的，每一门课程都要求自己开展独立研究项目作为期末考核标准。上课人数是小班教学，每门课的人数在2-6个学生，因此在上课的时候能够和教授进行积极的互动。虽然是文科，我们还可以选定自己感兴趣的研究小组，联系老师，进研究小组进行相关的课题研究。目前的服务状态是可以受理
编号为234的申请导师Sheila Zhu怎么样？编号为234的申请导师Sheila Zhu官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7062.html；简介：目前的服务状态是不合作
编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan怎么样？编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7055.html；简介：本科就读新加坡南洋理工大学电子与电机工程系，并以一等荣誉学位毕业；毕业后任职于世界500强企业，也是世界上最大的油田服务公司斯伦贝谢，从事项目管理相关工作；工作过程中想转行从事金融相关工作，就着手做了两件事，第一件事报考CFA，并在2018年通过三级考试并顺利持证；第二件事是申请金融相关的研究生，因为在海外时间比较长了，对申请学校也比较了解，所以是通过DIY的方式拿到了帝国理工（IC）、伦敦政经（LSE）以及伦敦大学学院（UCL）的offer并最终选择去帝国理工就读矿产与能源金融专业；研究生毕业后，经过一年的思考并了解各类金融相关工作，最终决定加入投资行业，并选择股权投资母基金这一细分领域，且很有幸的加入盈嘉资本担任投资经理一职。能为大家提供的帮助：1、在大学期间长期担任学生社团的管理层角色，且保持了相对高的成绩，对大学生活规划有独到的见解，可以帮助学生在入校之时就规划好大学四年的生活，例如如何在社团、实习、成绩间取舍。2、毕业后从石油行业逐步过渡到金融行业，对如何转行，尤其是非金融学生如何找到一份适合自己的金融工作有深刻的认识，并能根据学生情况给出具体可实施的计划、找到适合学生的岗位并对如何准备面试等具体事项提供帮助。3、因为从事股权投资行业，所以对当下热门的行业都有所了解，例如互联网、人工智能、半导体、先进制造等，对各行业未来的趋势看的相对清楚，结合自己多年的留学经历与海外工作经历，如果你对选学校选专业有困惑，以及对自身在现有行业内的发展路径不清晰，都可以帮你更好的做出决定。目前的服务状态是不合作

编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao怎么样？编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7061.html；简介：在香港一年多的时间，顺利完成学业，交友广泛，可以为学员分享香港tips和推荐稳定靠谱的房源！目前在国内top5综甲设计院工作～学长很爱交朋友，沉迷于音乐，本科时曾组建乐队，担任主音吉他手。日常会泡健身房，偶尔踢足球，喜欢旅行和摄影～学长从大四上拿了offer后，一直在做留学兼职，已成功帮多名学弟学妹拿到offer。非常熟悉香港，新加坡和英国的工科和商科专业的招生标准，申请流程，擅长为学生进行时间规划、择校和文书写作。除此之外，还可以指导学员进行背景提升、分享实习和求职经验。学员与我的关系不仅仅是服务和被服务，而是成为彼此相互信任的好友，学员入学后，在生活、学习、找实习、找工作时遇到问题都会找我咨询，我会用自己的经验和资源为学员指明方向～目前的服务状态是可以受理
编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan怎么样？编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7055.html；简介：本科就读新加坡南洋理工大学电子与电机工程系，并以一等荣誉学位毕业；毕业后任职于世界500强企业，也是世界上最大的油田服务公司斯伦贝谢，从事项目管理相关工作；工作过程中想转行从事金融相关工作，就着手做了两件事，第一件事报考CFA，并在2018年通过三级考试并顺利持证；第二件事是申请金融相关的研究生，因为在海外时间比较长了，对申请学校也比较了解，所以是通过DIY的方式拿到了帝国理工（IC）、伦敦政经（LSE）以及伦敦大学学院（UCL）的offer并最终选择去帝国理工就读矿产与能源金融专业；研究生毕业后，经过一年的思考并了解各类金融相关工作，最终决定加入投资行业，并选择股权投资母基金这一细分领域，且很有幸的加入盈嘉资本担任投资经理一职。能为大家提供的帮助：1、在大学期间长期担任学生社团的管理层角色，且保持了相对高的成绩，对大学生活规划有独到的见解，可以帮助学生在入校之时就规划好大学四年的生活，例如如何在社团、实习、成绩间取舍。2、毕业后从石油行业逐步过渡到金融行业，对如何转行，尤其是非金融学生如何找到一份适合自己的金融工作有深刻的认识，并能根据学生情况给出具体可实施的计划、找到适合学生的岗位并对如何准备面试等具体事项提供帮助。3、因为从事股权投资行业，所以对当下热门的行业都有所了解，例如互联网、人工智能、半导体、先进制造等，对各行业未来的趋势看的相对清楚，结合自己多年的留学经历与海外工作经历，如果你对选学校选专业有困惑，以及对自身在现有行业内的发展路径不清晰，都可以帮你更好的做出决定。目前的服务状态是不合作

编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan怎么样？编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7055.html；简介：本科就读新加坡南洋理工大学电子与电机工程系，并以一等荣誉学位毕业；毕业后任职于世界500强企业，也是世界上最大的油田服务公司斯伦贝谢，从事项目管理相关工作；工作过程中想转行从事金融相关工作，就着手做了两件事，第一件事报考CFA，并在2018年通过三级考试并顺利持证；第二件事是申请金融相关的研究生，因为在海外时间比较长了，对申请学校也比较了解，所以是通过DIY的方式拿到了帝国理工（IC）、伦敦政经（LSE）以及伦敦大学学院（UCL）的offer并最终选择去帝国理工就读矿产与能源金融专业；研究生毕业后，经过一年的思考并了解各类金融相关工作，最终决定加入投资行业，并选择股权投资母基金这一细分领域，且很有幸的加入盈嘉资本担任投资经理一职。能为大家提供的帮助：1、在大学期间长期担任学生社团的管理层角色，且保持了相对高的成绩，对大学生活规划有独到的见解，可以帮助学生在入校之时就规划好大学四年的生活，例如如何在社团、实习、成绩间取舍。2、毕业后从石油行业逐步过渡到金融行业，对如何转行，尤其是非金融学生如何找到一份适合自己的金融工作有深刻的认识，并能根据学生情况给出具体可实施的计划、找到适合学生的岗位并对如何准备面试等具体事项提供帮助。3、因为从事股权投资行业，所以对当下热门的行业都有所了解，例如互联网、人工智能、半导体、先进制造等，对各行业未来的趋势看的相对清楚，结合自己多年的留学经历与海外工作经历，如果你对选学校选专业有困惑，以及对自身在现有行业内的发展路径不清晰，都可以帮你更好的做出决定。目前的服务状态是不合作
编号为235的申请导师Xuecong Li 怎么样？编号为235的申请导师Xuecong Li 官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7054.html；简介：-目前的服务状态是不合作
编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang怎么样？编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7060.html；简介：拿到了香港城市大学（语言研究-翻译研究）/香港科技大学（中国文化）/比利时鲁汶大学(KU Leuven)（语言学高级硕士）/莱顿大学（语言学研究型硕士）/兰卡斯特大学（传播学）的offerIELTS （7.5），GPA: 3.3/4.0本身读的是汉语国际教育/英语，所以对语言学、应用语言学（对外汉语/对外汉语）、东亚语言文学、传播学、教育学有较多的了解现在在比利时的鲁汶，鲁汶是一个典型的欧洲大学城，几乎一半人口都是学生。目前的课程基本是深入的以研究为基础的，每一门课程都要求自己开展独立研究项目作为期末考核标准。上课人数是小班教学，每门课的人数在2-6个学生，因此在上课的时候能够和教授进行积极的互动。虽然是文科，我们还可以选定自己感兴趣的研究小组，联系老师，进研究小组进行相关的课题研究。目前的服务状态是可以受理
编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao怎么样？编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7061.html；简介：在香港一年多的时间，顺利完成学业，交友广泛，可以为学员分享香港tips和推荐稳定靠谱的房源！目前在国内top5综甲设计院工作～学长很爱交朋友，沉迷于音乐，本科时曾组建乐队，担任主音吉他手。日常会泡健身房，偶尔踢足球，喜欢旅行和摄影～学长从大四上拿了offer后，一直在做留学兼职，已成功帮多名学弟学妹拿到offer。非常熟悉香港，新加坡和英国的工科和商科专业的招生标准，申请流程，擅长为学生进行时间规划、择校和文书写作。除此之外，还可以指导学员进行背景提升、分享实习和求职经验。学员与我的关系不仅仅是服务和被服务，而是成为彼此相互信任的好友，学员入学后，在生活、学习、找实习、找工作时遇到问题都会找我咨询，我会用自己的经验和资源为学员指明方向～目前的服务状态是可以受理

编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan怎么样？编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7055.html；简介：本科就读新加坡南洋理工大学电子与电机工程系，并以一等荣誉学位毕业；毕业后任职于世界500强企业，也是世界上最大的油田服务公司斯伦贝谢，从事项目管理相关工作；工作过程中想转行从事金融相关工作，就着手做了两件事，第一件事报考CFA，并在2018年通过三级考试并顺利持证；第二件事是申请金融相关的研究生，因为在海外时间比较长了，对申请学校也比较了解，所以是通过DIY的方式拿到了帝国理工（IC）、伦敦政经（LSE）以及伦敦大学学院（UCL）的offer并最终选择去帝国理工就读矿产与能源金融专业；研究生毕业后，经过一年的思考并了解各类金融相关工作，最终决定加入投资行业，并选择股权投资母基金这一细分领域，且很有幸的加入盈嘉资本担任投资经理一职。能为大家提供的帮助：1、在大学期间长期担任学生社团的管理层角色，且保持了相对高的成绩，对大学生活规划有独到的见解，可以帮助学生在入校之时就规划好大学四年的生活，例如如何在社团、实习、成绩间取舍。2、毕业后从石油行业逐步过渡到金融行业，对如何转行，尤其是非金融学生如何找到一份适合自己的金融工作有深刻的认识，并能根据学生情况给出具体可实施的计划、找到适合学生的岗位并对如何准备面试等具体事项提供帮助。3、因为从事股权投资行业，所以对当下热门的行业都有所了解，例如互联网、人工智能、半导体、先进制造等，对各行业未来的趋势看的相对清楚，结合自己多年的留学经历与海外工作经历，如果你对选学校选专业有困惑，以及对自身在现有行业内的发展路径不清晰，都可以帮你更好的做出决定。目前的服务状态是不合作
编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao怎么样？编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7061.html；简介：在香港一年多的时间，顺利完成学业，交友广泛，可以为学员分享香港tips和推荐稳定靠谱的房源！目前在国内top5综甲设计院工作～学长很爱交朋友，沉迷于音乐，本科时曾组建乐队，担任主音吉他手。日常会泡健身房，偶尔踢足球，喜欢旅行和摄影～学长从大四上拿了offer后，一直在做留学兼职，已成功帮多名学弟学妹拿到offer。非常熟悉香港，新加坡和英国的工科和商科专业的招生标准，申请流程，擅长为学生进行时间规划、择校和文书写作。除此之外，还可以指导学员进行背景提升、分享实习和求职经验。学员与我的关系不仅仅是服务和被服务，而是成为彼此相互信任的好友，学员入学后，在生活、学习、找实习、找工作时遇到问题都会找我咨询，我会用自己的经验和资源为学员指明方向～目前的服务状态是可以受理

编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang怎么样？编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7060.html；简介：拿到了香港城市大学（语言研究-翻译研究）/香港科技大学（中国文化）/比利时鲁汶大学(KU Leuven)（语言学高级硕士）/莱顿大学（语言学研究型硕士）/兰卡斯特大学（传播学）的offerIELTS （7.5），GPA: 3.3/4.0本身读的是汉语国际教育/英语，所以对语言学、应用语言学（对外汉语/对外汉语）、东亚语言文学、传播学、教育学有较多的了解现在在比利时的鲁汶，鲁汶是一个典型的欧洲大学城，几乎一半人口都是学生。目前的课程基本是深入的以研究为基础的，每一门课程都要求自己开展独立研究项目作为期末考核标准。上课人数是小班教学，每门课的人数在2-6个学生，因此在上课的时候能够和教授进行积极的互动。虽然是文科，我们还可以选定自己感兴趣的研究小组，联系老师，进研究小组进行相关的课题研究。目前的服务状态是可以受理
编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan怎么样？编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7055.html；简介：本科就读新加坡南洋理工大学电子与电机工程系，并以一等荣誉学位毕业；毕业后任职于世界500强企业，也是世界上最大的油田服务公司斯伦贝谢，从事项目管理相关工作；工作过程中想转行从事金融相关工作，就着手做了两件事，第一件事报考CFA，并在2018年通过三级考试并顺利持证；第二件事是申请金融相关的研究生，因为在海外时间比较长了，对申请学校也比较了解，所以是通过DIY的方式拿到了帝国理工（IC）、伦敦政经（LSE）以及伦敦大学学院（UCL）的offer并最终选择去帝国理工就读矿产与能源金融专业；研究生毕业后，经过一年的思考并了解各类金融相关工作，最终决定加入投资行业，并选择股权投资母基金这一细分领域，且很有幸的加入盈嘉资本担任投资经理一职。能为大家提供的帮助：1、在大学期间长期担任学生社团的管理层角色，且保持了相对高的成绩，对大学生活规划有独到的见解，可以帮助学生在入校之时就规划好大学四年的生活，例如如何在社团、实习、成绩间取舍。2、毕业后从石油行业逐步过渡到金融行业，对如何转行，尤其是非金融学生如何找到一份适合自己的金融工作有深刻的认识，并能根据学生情况给出具体可实施的计划、找到适合学生的岗位并对如何准备面试等具体事项提供帮助。3、因为从事股权投资行业，所以对当下热门的行业都有所了解，例如互联网、人工智能、半导体、先进制造等，对各行业未来的趋势看的相对清楚，结合自己多年的留学经历与海外工作经历，如果你对选学校选专业有困惑，以及对自身在现有行业内的发展路径不清晰，都可以帮你更好的做出决定。目前的服务状态是不合作
编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao怎么样？编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7061.html；简介：在香港一年多的时间，顺利完成学业，交友广泛，可以为学员分享香港tips和推荐稳定靠谱的房源！目前在国内top5综甲设计院工作～学长很爱交朋友，沉迷于音乐，本科时曾组建乐队，担任主音吉他手。日常会泡健身房，偶尔踢足球，喜欢旅行和摄影～学长从大四上拿了offer后，一直在做留学兼职，已成功帮多名学弟学妹拿到offer。非常熟悉香港，新加坡和英国的工科和商科专业的招生标准，申请流程，擅长为学生进行时间规划、择校和文书写作。除此之外，还可以指导学员进行背景提升、分享实习和求职经验。学员与我的关系不仅仅是服务和被服务，而是成为彼此相互信任的好友，学员入学后，在生活、学习、找实习、找工作时遇到问题都会找我咨询，我会用自己的经验和资源为学员指明方向～目前的服务状态是可以受理

编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang怎么样？编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7060.html；简介：拿到了香港城市大学（语言研究-翻译研究）/香港科技大学（中国文化）/比利时鲁汶大学(KU Leuven)（语言学高级硕士）/莱顿大学（语言学研究型硕士）/兰卡斯特大学（传播学）的offerIELTS （7.5），GPA: 3.3/4.0本身读的是汉语国际教育/英语，所以对语言学、应用语言学（对外汉语/对外汉语）、东亚语言文学、传播学、教育学有较多的了解现在在比利时的鲁汶，鲁汶是一个典型的欧洲大学城，几乎一半人口都是学生。目前的课程基本是深入的以研究为基础的，每一门课程都要求自己开展独立研究项目作为期末考核标准。上课人数是小班教学，每门课的人数在2-6个学生，因此在上课的时候能够和教授进行积极的互动。虽然是文科，我们还可以选定自己感兴趣的研究小组，联系老师，进研究小组进行相关的课题研究。目前的服务状态是可以受理
编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan怎么样？编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7055.html；简介：本科就读新加坡南洋理工大学电子与电机工程系，并以一等荣誉学位毕业；毕业后任职于世界500强企业，也是世界上最大的油田服务公司斯伦贝谢，从事项目管理相关工作；工作过程中想转行从事金融相关工作，就着手做了两件事，第一件事报考CFA，并在2018年通过三级考试并顺利持证；第二件事是申请金融相关的研究生，因为在海外时间比较长了，对申请学校也比较了解，所以是通过DIY的方式拿到了帝国理工（IC）、伦敦政经（LSE）以及伦敦大学学院（UCL）的offer并最终选择去帝国理工就读矿产与能源金融专业；研究生毕业后，经过一年的思考并了解各类金融相关工作，最终决定加入投资行业，并选择股权投资母基金这一细分领域，且很有幸的加入盈嘉资本担任投资经理一职。能为大家提供的帮助：1、在大学期间长期担任学生社团的管理层角色，且保持了相对高的成绩，对大学生活规划有独到的见解，可以帮助学生在入校之时就规划好大学四年的生活，例如如何在社团、实习、成绩间取舍。2、毕业后从石油行业逐步过渡到金融行业，对如何转行，尤其是非金融学生如何找到一份适合自己的金融工作有深刻的认识，并能根据学生情况给出具体可实施的计划、找到适合学生的岗位并对如何准备面试等具体事项提供帮助。3、因为从事股权投资行业，所以对当下热门的行业都有所了解，例如互联网、人工智能、半导体、先进制造等，对各行业未来的趋势看的相对清楚，结合自己多年的留学经历与海外工作经历，如果你对选学校选专业有困惑，以及对自身在现有行业内的发展路径不清晰，都可以帮你更好的做出决定。目前的服务状态是不合作
编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao怎么样？编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7061.html；简介：在香港一年多的时间，顺利完成学业，交友广泛，可以为学员分享香港tips和推荐稳定靠谱的房源！目前在国内top5综甲设计院工作～学长很爱交朋友，沉迷于音乐，本科时曾组建乐队，担任主音吉他手。日常会泡健身房，偶尔踢足球，喜欢旅行和摄影～学长从大四上拿了offer后，一直在做留学兼职，已成功帮多名学弟学妹拿到offer。非常熟悉香港，新加坡和英国的工科和商科专业的招生标准，申请流程，擅长为学生进行时间规划、择校和文书写作。除此之外，还可以指导学员进行背景提升、分享实习和求职经验。学员与我的关系不仅仅是服务和被服务，而是成为彼此相互信任的好友，学员入学后，在生活、学习、找实习、找工作时遇到问题都会找我咨询，我会用自己的经验和资源为学员指明方向～目前的服务状态是可以受理
编号为240的申请导师Jason Osborne的教育经历是什么？就读学校：北卡罗来纳大学教堂山分校、就读专业跨学科研究：文化研究、学位文学学士| Bachelor of Arts|B.A.，入学日期2003-09-01、毕业日期2009-07-31，均分，GPA分，，学业状态毕业，该学位是否为目前最高学历：否。

编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan怎么样？编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7055.html；简介：本科就读新加坡南洋理工大学电子与电机工程系，并以一等荣誉学位毕业；毕业后任职于世界500强企业，也是世界上最大的油田服务公司斯伦贝谢，从事项目管理相关工作；工作过程中想转行从事金融相关工作，就着手做了两件事，第一件事报考CFA，并在2018年通过三级考试并顺利持证；第二件事是申请金融相关的研究生，因为在海外时间比较长了，对申请学校也比较了解，所以是通过DIY的方式拿到了帝国理工（IC）、伦敦政经（LSE）以及伦敦大学学院（UCL）的offer并最终选择去帝国理工就读矿产与能源金融专业；研究生毕业后，经过一年的思考并了解各类金融相关工作，最终决定加入投资行业，并选择股权投资母基金这一细分领域，且很有幸的加入盈嘉资本担任投资经理一职。能为大家提供的帮助：1、在大学期间长期担任学生社团的管理层角色，且保持了相对高的成绩，对大学生活规划有独到的见解，可以帮助学生在入校之时就规划好大学四年的生活，例如如何在社团、实习、成绩间取舍。2、毕业后从石油行业逐步过渡到金融行业，对如何转行，尤其是非金融学生如何找到一份适合自己的金融工作有深刻的认识，并能根据学生情况给出具体可实施的计划、找到适合学生的岗位并对如何准备面试等具体事项提供帮助。3、因为从事股权投资行业，所以对当下热门的行业都有所了解，例如互联网、人工智能、半导体、先进制造等，对各行业未来的趋势看的相对清楚，结合自己多年的留学经历与海外工作经历，如果你对选学校选专业有困惑，以及对自身在现有行业内的发展路径不清晰，都可以帮你更好的做出决定。目前的服务状态是不合作

编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang怎么样？编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7060.html；简介：拿到了香港城市大学（语言研究-翻译研究）/香港科技大学（中国文化）/比利时鲁汶大学(KU Leuven)（语言学高级硕士）/莱顿大学（语言学研究型硕士）/兰卡斯特大学（传播学）的offerIELTS （7.5），GPA: 3.3/4.0本身读的是汉语国际教育/英语，所以对语言学、应用语言学（对外汉语/对外汉语）、东亚语言文学、传播学、教育学有较多的了解现在在比利时的鲁汶，鲁汶是一个典型的欧洲大学城，几乎一半人口都是学生。目前的课程基本是深入的以研究为基础的，每一门课程都要求自己开展独立研究项目作为期末考核标准。上课人数是小班教学，每门课的人数在2-6个学生，因此在上课的时候能够和教授进行积极的互动。虽然是文科，我们还可以选定自己感兴趣的研究小组，联系老师，进研究小组进行相关的课题研究。目前的服务状态是可以受理

编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao怎么样？编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7061.html；简介：在香港一年多的时间，顺利完成学业，交友广泛，可以为学员分享香港tips和推荐稳定靠谱的房源！目前在国内top5综甲设计院工作～学长很爱交朋友，沉迷于音乐，本科时曾组建乐队，担任主音吉他手。日常会泡健身房，偶尔踢足球，喜欢旅行和摄影～学长从大四上拿了offer后，一直在做留学兼职，已成功帮多名学弟学妹拿到offer。非常熟悉香港，新加坡和英国的工科和商科专业的招生标准，申请流程，擅长为学生进行时间规划、择校和文书写作。除此之外，还可以指导学员进行背景提升、分享实习和求职经验。学员与我的关系不仅仅是服务和被服务，而是成为彼此相互信任的好友，学员入学后，在生活、学习、找实习、找工作时遇到问题都会找我咨询，我会用自己的经验和资源为学员指明方向～目前的服务状态是可以受理
编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang怎么样？编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7060.html；简介：拿到了香港城市大学（语言研究-翻译研究）/香港科技大学（中国文化）/比利时鲁汶大学(KU Leuven)（语言学高级硕士）/莱顿大学（语言学研究型硕士）/兰卡斯特大学（传播学）的offerIELTS （7.5），GPA: 3.3/4.0本身读的是汉语国际教育/英语，所以对语言学、应用语言学（对外汉语/对外汉语）、东亚语言文学、传播学、教育学有较多的了解现在在比利时的鲁汶，鲁汶是一个典型的欧洲大学城，几乎一半人口都是学生。目前的课程基本是深入的以研究为基础的，每一门课程都要求自己开展独立研究项目作为期末考核标准。上课人数是小班教学，每门课的人数在2-6个学生，因此在上课的时候能够和教授进行积极的互动。虽然是文科，我们还可以选定自己感兴趣的研究小组，联系老师，进研究小组进行相关的课题研究。目前的服务状态是可以受理
编号为234的申请导师Sheila Zhu怎么样？编号为234的申请导师Sheila Zhu官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7062.html；简介：目前的服务状态是不合作
编号为235的申请导师Xuecong Li 怎么样？编号为235的申请导师Xuecong Li 官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7054.html；简介：-目前的服务状态是不合作
编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan怎么样？编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7055.html；简介：本科就读新加坡南洋理工大学电子与电机工程系，并以一等荣誉学位毕业；毕业后任职于世界500强企业，也是世界上最大的油田服务公司斯伦贝谢，从事项目管理相关工作；工作过程中想转行从事金融相关工作，就着手做了两件事，第一件事报考CFA，并在2018年通过三级考试并顺利持证；第二件事是申请金融相关的研究生，因为在海外时间比较长了，对申请学校也比较了解，所以是通过DIY的方式拿到了帝国理工（IC）、伦敦政经（LSE）以及伦敦大学学院（UCL）的offer并最终选择去帝国理工就读矿产与能源金融专业；研究生毕业后，经过一年的思考并了解各类金融相关工作，最终决定加入投资行业，并选择股权投资母基金这一细分领域，且很有幸的加入盈嘉资本担任投资经理一职。能为大家提供的帮助：1、在大学期间长期担任学生社团的管理层角色，且保持了相对高的成绩，对大学生活规划有独到的见解，可以帮助学生在入校之时就规划好大学四年的生活，例如如何在社团、实习、成绩间取舍。2、毕业后从石油行业逐步过渡到金融行业，对如何转行，尤其是非金融学生如何找到一份适合自己的金融工作有深刻的认识，并能根据学生情况给出具体可实施的计划、找到适合学生的岗位并对如何准备面试等具体事项提供帮助。3、因为从事股权投资行业，所以对当下热门的行业都有所了解，例如互联网、人工智能、半导体、先进制造等，对各行业未来的趋势看的相对清楚，结合自己多年的留学经历与海外工作经历，如果你对选学校选专业有困惑，以及对自身在现有行业内的发展路径不清晰，都可以帮你更好的做出决定。目前的服务状态是不合作

编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao怎么样？编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7061.html；简介：在香港一年多的时间，顺利完成学业，交友广泛，可以为学员分享香港tips和推荐稳定靠谱的房源！目前在国内top5综甲设计院工作～学长很爱交朋友，沉迷于音乐，本科时曾组建乐队，担任主音吉他手。日常会泡健身房，偶尔踢足球，喜欢旅行和摄影～学长从大四上拿了offer后，一直在做留学兼职，已成功帮多名学弟学妹拿到offer。非常熟悉香港，新加坡和英国的工科和商科专业的招生标准，申请流程，擅长为学生进行时间规划、择校和文书写作。除此之外，还可以指导学员进行背景提升、分享实习和求职经验。学员与我的关系不仅仅是服务和被服务，而是成为彼此相互信任的好友，学员入学后，在生活、学习、找实习、找工作时遇到问题都会找我咨询，我会用自己的经验和资源为学员指明方向～目前的服务状态是可以受理
编号为234的申请导师Sheila Zhu怎么样？编号为234的申请导师Sheila Zhu官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7062.html；简介：目前的服务状态是不合作
编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan怎么样？编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7055.html；简介：本科就读新加坡南洋理工大学电子与电机工程系，并以一等荣誉学位毕业；毕业后任职于世界500强企业，也是世界上最大的油田服务公司斯伦贝谢，从事项目管理相关工作；工作过程中想转行从事金融相关工作，就着手做了两件事，第一件事报考CFA，并在2018年通过三级考试并顺利持证；第二件事是申请金融相关的研究生，因为在海外时间比较长了，对申请学校也比较了解，所以是通过DIY的方式拿到了帝国理工（IC）、伦敦政经（LSE）以及伦敦大学学院（UCL）的offer并最终选择去帝国理工就读矿产与能源金融专业；研究生毕业后，经过一年的思考并了解各类金融相关工作，最终决定加入投资行业，并选择股权投资母基金这一细分领域，且很有幸的加入盈嘉资本担任投资经理一职。能为大家提供的帮助：1、在大学期间长期担任学生社团的管理层角色，且保持了相对高的成绩，对大学生活规划有独到的见解，可以帮助学生在入校之时就规划好大学四年的生活，例如如何在社团、实习、成绩间取舍。2、毕业后从石油行业逐步过渡到金融行业，对如何转行，尤其是非金融学生如何找到一份适合自己的金融工作有深刻的认识，并能根据学生情况给出具体可实施的计划、找到适合学生的岗位并对如何准备面试等具体事项提供帮助。3、因为从事股权投资行业，所以对当下热门的行业都有所了解，例如互联网、人工智能、半导体、先进制造等，对各行业未来的趋势看的相对清楚，结合自己多年的留学经历与海外工作经历，如果你对选学校选专业有困惑，以及对自身在现有行业内的发展路径不清晰，都可以帮你更好的做出决定。目前的服务状态是不合作

编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang怎么样？编号为238的申请导师Samuel Yang官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7060.html；简介：拿到了香港城市大学（语言研究-翻译研究）/香港科技大学（中国文化）/比利时鲁汶大学(KU Leuven)（语言学高级硕士）/莱顿大学（语言学研究型硕士）/兰卡斯特大学（传播学）的offerIELTS （7.5），GPA: 3.3/4.0本身读的是汉语国际教育/英语，所以对语言学、应用语言学（对外汉语/对外汉语）、东亚语言文学、传播学、教育学有较多的了解现在在比利时的鲁汶，鲁汶是一个典型的欧洲大学城，几乎一半人口都是学生。目前的课程基本是深入的以研究为基础的，每一门课程都要求自己开展独立研究项目作为期末考核标准。上课人数是小班教学，每门课的人数在2-6个学生，因此在上课的时候能够和教授进行积极的互动。虽然是文科，我们还可以选定自己感兴趣的研究小组，联系老师，进研究小组进行相关的课题研究。目前的服务状态是可以受理

编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan怎么样？编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7055.html；简介：本科就读新加坡南洋理工大学电子与电机工程系，并以一等荣誉学位毕业；毕业后任职于世界500强企业，也是世界上最大的油田服务公司斯伦贝谢，从事项目管理相关工作；工作过程中想转行从事金融相关工作，就着手做了两件事，第一件事报考CFA，并在2018年通过三级考试并顺利持证；第二件事是申请金融相关的研究生，因为在海外时间比较长了，对申请学校也比较了解，所以是通过DIY的方式拿到了帝国理工（IC）、伦敦政经（LSE）以及伦敦大学学院（UCL）的offer并最终选择去帝国理工就读矿产与能源金融专业；研究生毕业后，经过一年的思考并了解各类金融相关工作，最终决定加入投资行业，并选择股权投资母基金这一细分领域，且很有幸的加入盈嘉资本担任投资经理一职。能为大家提供的帮助：1、在大学期间长期担任学生社团的管理层角色，且保持了相对高的成绩，对大学生活规划有独到的见解，可以帮助学生在入校之时就规划好大学四年的生活，例如如何在社团、实习、成绩间取舍。2、毕业后从石油行业逐步过渡到金融行业，对如何转行，尤其是非金融学生如何找到一份适合自己的金融工作有深刻的认识，并能根据学生情况给出具体可实施的计划、找到适合学生的岗位并对如何准备面试等具体事项提供帮助。3、因为从事股权投资行业，所以对当下热门的行业都有所了解，例如互联网、人工智能、半导体、先进制造等，对各行业未来的趋势看的相对清楚，结合自己多年的留学经历与海外工作经历，如果你对选学校选专业有困惑，以及对自身在现有行业内的发展路径不清晰，都可以帮你更好的做出决定。目前的服务状态是不合作

编号为237的申请导师Pofee Zhao的教育经历是什么？就读学校：天津大学、就读专业土木工程、学位工学学士| Bachelor of Engineering|B.Eng.，入学日期2013-09-01、毕业日期2017-07-01，均分，GPA分，，学业状态毕业，该学位是否为目前最高学历：否。
学员背景：2教育经历：2011-09-01至2015-06-30就读，均分，GPA3.46/4，After I started my undergraduate study in Jinan University and graduate study at Hong Kong Polytechnic University, I have taken many steps (both academic and practical) to quest a clear career advancement in Investor Relations (IR) fields. My current career goal of entering Tencent as an Investor Relations Manager stems from my 4 yrs working experience at IR & PR firms, in which I have been extensively exposed to the wants-and-needs of listed firms in terms of their capital market presences. Specifically, by engaging in intensive real business practice and by consciously maintaining intimate relationships with listed firms in HK, I availed myself of IR working methodologies and relation maintaining technics.When it comes to my professional exposures, my working experiences at IR agencies really armed me with critical understanding about IR working flow. I had decent practice on stock price analysis, equity research analysis, competitive analysis and logistic works such as investor meeting arrangement, seasonal reports releasing, Q&A simulation etc. But again, I would love to join a large market cap firm, in which IR staffs have more exposures to financial modelling, high profile investor network and quantitative analysis.However, I could see bottlenecks holding me back from chasing my career goal of joining Tencent IR. Firstly, as the leading firm in TMT sector globally, Tencent sets up a relatively high recruitment standard for its IR position, supposedly a candidate with a well-known MBA background in a prestigious University such as HKU would be preferred. Secondly, in large cap listed companies such as Tencent, departmental head in IR is often equipped with a Finance plus MBA degree. Given my academic major is not finance, and the schools I graduated from are not world-class, so the recruiters may question my professional skills and network outreach. At the same time, I don't want to face the bottleneck of promotion in the future.My initial consideration of applying for an esteemed MBA program comes along with the book <Principles> written by Ray Dalio, among all those insightful contents, one sentence impressed me most, “Meaningful work and meaningful relationships were and still are my primary goals and everything I did was for them”. So career-wise, to become an excellent IR executive, I should be equipped with enough capital markets knowledge base, problem solving techniques, and a good command of the macroeconomic situation/capital trends. But unfortunately most of this knowledge is not involved in undergrad and graduate studies, so I really need an MBA opportunity to enrich my knowledge reserve by diving into the core courses such as Accounting for Business Decisions, Analytics for Managers, Corporate Finance and Competitive Strategy; moreover, I can also leverage on the electives such as Consulting&Stratrgy to compensate my own interest.Driven by seeking for “meaningful work (quote Ray Dalio)” and knowledge base, one of the most exciting part of the HKU MBA program for me lies in the course structure combined with business lab which makes the learning process more practical and logical. Particularly, given my knowledge absorptive capacity is, to a great extent, based on my fast-learning and self-learning abilities, so the core lessons, workshops and innovative elective lectures combined will undoubtedly consolidate my qualitative-based and quantitative-focused expertise, efficiently bridging my knowledge reserve from a Bachelor in Business English to a MBA candidate in HKU from shallow to deep, from scattered to holistic panorama. And HKU MBA is differentiated from other MBA programmes in Hong Kong because of its flexibility to choose “weekday mode” and “weekend day mode”, by taking this advantage I can better balance my life, job hunting and pedagogical pace.“Meaningful relationships (quote Ray Dalio)” are very essential both for job hunting and for building a sustainable and successful career. I firmly reckon that HKEX listed firms’ attention would chase HKU’s endorsements: such as itsworld-standard prestige, bright peers, and career service supports, etc. Engaging in HKU Career Service would be a state-of-the-art approach to obtain insider views and networks from outstanding alumni. Drawing on HKU’s world-class finance faculty and thought-leaders in capital market, corporate management and technology, the programme provides a unique perspective of business — one where business fundamentals intersect with the latest in technology and innovation, and where management science is blended with data-driven decision making. Moreover, HKU’s partnerships with London Business School and Columbia Business School provide students with unparalleled educational and networking opportunities. And based on my own observations, I could definitely benefit from the international experience, outstanding alum network and state-of-the-art knowledge of global business dynamics.With the foresight of HKU faculty, I would definitely become an intelligent IR executive and as well as a socially conscientious person. My previous engagement at IR agencies granted me the experiences of serving 100+ firms with their IR needs. I believe my time and passion devoted into HKU would certainly inject more cultural vigor to diversify the campus community and would bring about promising bilateral returns in the foreseeable future.

学员背景：1教育经历：2006-09-01至2010-06-25就读成都理工大学核工程与核技术工It was a huge decision in my life. I majored in nuclear engineering and technology in my bachelor’s study. After working in that industry for years after graduation, I switched gears and headed into the world of social science, practicing in early childhood education. This was a decision that formed over time, and it was also influenced by my family and some great acquaintances through the way. Now as I am applying for the Master of Science in Psychological Studies (Conversion) program at the University of Glasgow, I am very eager to join an academic community with the shared enthusiasm and passion for the course, and I also believe that the study and experience at your program would provide me with necessary knowledge to step up in my future career, both as a practitioner and a researcher in the field of psychology and education.My original area of study and work, working as an engineer at a state agency, was stable and paid off. It was perfect according to my parents’ expectations and it would have been a secure job desired by many, but not for me. Throughout the years, I gradually came to the realization that this was not a position that could fulfill my personal values and life goals. Although I did not fully agree with my parents’ expectations for my career, there is no doubt that they influenced me greatly growing up. Both my mother and my father put great passion and respect into their jobs, and watching them doing so has always motivated me to find my real fitful position in the society and contribute to it through my work. Then, I had the experience of going to counselling sessions, which were not and are not common in China, and I started to try to discover and understand myself with the help of the counsellor. I was amazed by how the sessions had changed my view and way of thinking and thankful to how the counsellor encouraged me to dedicate more to self-betterment and self-realization. These two factors inspired me to become a person that can appreciate people, help people, and change people’s lives to be better.Understanding that I will have to work twice as hard to prepare myself for a drastic career change, I enrolled in sociology and psychology certificate courses to enrich me with a theoretical basis. The first certificate course I took was at Renmin University of China, and it gave me the first glimpse of areas like gender studies, collective psychology, and social psychology. Then as I endeavored deeper through more reading and another online psychology course, I increasingly realized that people were sculpted from the earliest words from parents to the general social environment that was inevitable to all of us, and starting a career that could touch the deepest part inside a person would absolutely be my dream. It also came to my realization that to truly step into this field, I need to get practical experiences to test my new knowledge and develop myself through the way. So, I quitted my old job and became an early childhood teacher at Gymboree Early Childhood Development Center in Beijing.In that position, I sensed great challenges from the very beginning. Working for 50 hours per week, I had to prepare all-English lesson plans, teach various bilingual courses (play, music, art course, etc.) to children of seven different age levels, take professional training, and communicate with parents for their questions and concerns. It was very rewarding to be sure; I was able to meet children of all different personalities and backgrounds. Observing their behaviors and interactions with parents in my class was especially fascinating. Each one of them exhibited unique developmental progress and reflected the influence from family, peers, and society, and it was my responsibility to design scaffolded layers for classroom activities considering all of their attributes. It was particularly motivating to be able to use the knowledge I learned in the certificate course and online course in my practice. For instance,using the zone of proximal development in developmental psychology, I was always able to challenge the children while ensuring their completion and acquisition in the activities. Through this job, I had a deeper understanding of the physical, cognitive, and emotional development of children, and I also found out that it was very crucial to use psychological methods to understand the behaviors and thoughts of children. Only when they are broken down into meaningful interpretations can I better assist the children with their growth. Also, for the parents, having a solid psychological background is the premise for me to provide concrete and effective suggestions to them on how to better interact with their children, but as I sometimes found it hard to provide more professional answers to the parents’ questions, concerns and anxiety which makes me feel helpless and frustrated, I also became aware of my limitations and needs for more theoretical support.Studying in the Master of Science in Psychological Studies (Conversion) program will be the step I have to take in my career. The Chinese society is going through immense changes and people are more aware of the importance of mental health, and the scenario is even more so in educational settings. Due to test-oriented education and more fierce competition in their future careers, Chinese students of all ages go through accumulating stress from schools, families, and other uncertainties. When I finish the study at your program, I intend to continue working in the education field, assisting both children and parents to deal with mental issues and construct a healthy environment for all kids to nourish. Because I did not have a long-time systematic training on psychology, the extensive coursework in the fundamental and specialized psychological theories is a great introduction for me to really get into this field. The specific courses about educational psychology, developmental issues, and professional skills contribute even more to my planned future career path. I am certain that if I could have the honor to study at the University of Glasgow, I will become a more competent practitioner, a more erudite researcher, and a more capable person who can touch the lives of more people and make them for the better, just as I envisioned when I “switched the gear.”Thank you very much for your time and consideration.
