学员背景：1教育经历：至就读加州大学圣塔芭芭拉分校风险管理与金融工程，均分，GPA3.10/4，In the future, I see myself as a successful portfolio manager in a hedge fund managing millions of AUM. My career goal was first motivated by my father’s success story as a business investor and his decision to immigrate to Hong Kong through financial investments. I am deeply attracted to the process of identifying profitable opportunities and diversifying idiosyncratic risk through portfolio investments. Therefore, as a statistics student, I set high goals to become a portfolio manager bringing finance and data analytics together to create brilliant outgrowth benefiting society. This constitutes the impetus to pursue my dream program, the MSc in Financial Technology at HKUST.To prepare for the FinTech program, I have developed a solid quantitative academic background with a bachelor of Applied Statistics at the University of California, Santa Barbara (UCSB). I gained excellent quantitative skills in my Mathematics and Statistics courses like Time Series, Regression Analysis, Probability and Statistics, and acquired advanced programming skills in R, SAS, Python, and C++ Programming. I also nurtured my leadership skills in a Social Campaign Project to promote the UCSB Counseling & Psychological Services by making campaign videos, social media leaflets, and websites. In this project, I led a team of six members and allocated tasks like video filming, poster design, and web building based on their individual talents and interests. To hone my business abilities, I also equipped myself with basic entrepreneurship and management knowledge through Business Proposal Writing. In this proposal, I completed a business plan of a basketball club to provide a platform for members to exchange ideas and skills after referring to over 30 existing club proposals. I believe I am well prepared to continue my graduate study in the financial technology field and pursue my career to manage a hedge fund.To enhance my problem-solving skills, I applied my quantitative skills to research and professional projects. In 2019, through a “Forecast Monthly Traffic Fatalities using methods of Time Series Analysis” research project, I gained hands-on experience in big data analysis. To construct a model that reduces the death rate due to traffic accidents in the United States, I transformed and differenced the data related to traffic fatalities. I then built on this new dataset two candidate Seasonal Autoregressive Integrated Moving Average (SARIMA) models: SARIMA(5,0,0) x (0,1,1)12, SARIMA(5,0,0) x (3,1,0)12. After comparing their respective AICs, checking casual and invertibility, residual plots, diagnostic checking, I select SARIMA(5,0,0) x (3,1,0)12 as my final model used for forecasting. Based on the final model forecast for the traffic fatalities from January 1974 to December 1974, I found that the true values are in the 95% confidence interval of my predicted data. This model forecasting traffic fatality would benefit businesses of various kinds. For example, insurance companies may adjust their actuarial assumptions. Automobile companies may improve their vehicle designs. And government agents may also optimize their infrastructure plans according to the predictions of my model. Thanks to this experience, I explored various statistical and visualization tools and realized the power of analytics in enhancing business decision-making. Thus, my analytics skills will prepare me for my graduate study in the HKUSTMScFinTech program.Craving more experiences in the financial industry, I decided to explore the professional environment through internships. As a sales and trading intern at Bosera Asset Management, I mainly focused on the public offering of Bosera Central-SOEs’ Structural Reform Index ETF. To convince our clients, I prepared a comprehensive due diligence report covering 100 component stocks, detailing their respective portfolio weights and investment information. To further illustrate the competitive advantages, I web-scripted all the 140 comparable index funds on the market and summarized the advantages and disadvantages of each ETF. My summary reports have greatly facilitated my team’s working efficiency and were praised by my supervisor. In another investment banking division (IBD) internship in China Securities, I assisted in the due diligence process of the initial public offering (IPO) of a municipal investment group. I manually checked and summarized all the municipal IPOs rejection reasons by the SEC, applied the Politics, Economy, Society, Technology (PEST) analytical framework, and employed the SWOT analysis to gain a comprehensive and unbiased risk assessment on the underlying asset. Furthermore, I augmented risk information such as ownership change, restriction on sales, and collateral conditions with alternative online sources including qichacha.com and Eastmoney.com. Realizing the huge amount of labor work for due diligence, I believe that the trending machine learning and big data techniques can greatly reform the whole portfolio management industry by automating redundant processes. For example, the core courses such as Financial Data Mining and AI for FinTech shall equip me with various deep learning architectures to simplify most of the inefficient work. The intrinsic joy I can obtain from applying financial technology to generate revenue further strengthens my career goal as a portfolio manager.Based on these experiences, I have developed a clear career plan to achieve my dream as a portfolio manager. At HKUST, I would like to gain expertise in innovative financial technology through elective courses like Cryptocurrency, Blockchain, and Their Business Applications, as well as FinTech and Big Data Financial Analytics. Upon graduation, I would like to launch my career as a financial analyst in sell-side banks and jump to buy-side hedge funds within three years. In the long run, I envision incorporating analytics, finance and management skills into portfolio management. Hence, the MScFinTech program at HKUST stands out to me for three reasons. Firstly, its emphasis on interdisciplinary skills in statistics, engineering, and financial principles would greatly stimulate my innovative solutions in addressing complex big data problems. Secondly, the program’s rigorous training and state-of-art curriculum would enable me to capture frontier knowledge of information technology, blockchain, decision analytics. Lastly, HKUST’s strong alumni network in Greater China attracts to me, as it would assist me with both my immediate career as a financial analyst and my long-term career as a portfolio manager. With the MSc in Financial Technology from HKUST, I would definitely achieve successful career growth to operate a hedge fund, support more business in achieving their goals, and also utilize my resources to contribute to HKUST and society in the future.

编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan怎么样？编号为236的申请导师Yiqun Huan官网展示链接地址：https://www.wordsunny.com/tutorListDetail-7055.html；简介：本科就读新加坡南洋理工大学电子与电机工程系，并以一等荣誉学位毕业；毕业后任职于世界500强企业，也是世界上最大的油田服务公司斯伦贝谢，从事项目管理相关工作；工作过程中想转行从事金融相关工作，就着手做了两件事，第一件事报考CFA，并在2018年通过三级考试并顺利持证；第二件事是申请金融相关的研究生，因为在海外时间比较长了，对申请学校也比较了解，所以是通过DIY的方式拿到了帝国理工（IC）、伦敦政经（LSE）以及伦敦大学学院（UCL）的offer并最终选择去帝国理工就读矿产与能源金融专业；研究生毕业后，经过一年的思考并了解各类金融相关工作，最终决定加入投资行业，并选择股权投资母基金这一细分领域，且很有幸的加入盈嘉资本担任投资经理一职。能为大家提供的帮助：1、在大学期间长期担任学生社团的管理层角色，且保持了相对高的成绩，对大学生活规划有独到的见解，可以帮助学生在入校之时就规划好大学四年的生活，例如如何在社团、实习、成绩间取舍。2、毕业后从石油行业逐步过渡到金融行业，对如何转行，尤其是非金融学生如何找到一份适合自己的金融工作有深刻的认识，并能根据学生情况给出具体可实施的计划、找到适合学生的岗位并对如何准备面试等具体事项提供帮助。3、因为从事股权投资行业，所以对当下热门的行业都有所了解，例如互联网、人工智能、半导体、先进制造等，对各行业未来的趋势看的相对清楚，结合自己多年的留学经历与海外工作经历，如果你对选学校选专业有困惑，以及对自身在现有行业内的发展路径不清晰，都可以帮你更好的做出决定。目前的服务状态是不合作
